Part 1 
【当季新题】2026 年01-04 月Part 1 正式题库和解析 
Dreams 
Question 1: 
Can you remember the dreams you had? 
Useful phrases: 
vivid dreams 生动的梦 
fade quickly 很快消失 
strange details 奇怪的细节 
Sample answer: 
I can sometimes remember my dreams, especially when they are vivid or emotional. However, most of the 
time they fade quickly after I wake up, and only a few strange details stay in my mind. I usually forget them 
completely by the time I start my day. 
Question 2: 
Do you share your dreams with others? 
Useful phrases: 
close friends 亲密朋友 
keep it private 保持私密 
feel understood 被理解 
Sample answer: 
I don’t usually share my dreams with many people, only with close friends or family members. Some dreams 
feel too personal, so I prefer to keep them private unless I really trust someone. When I do share them, it 
makes me feel understood and supported. 
Question 3 
Do you think dreams have special meanings? 
Useful phrases: 
reflect emotions 反映情绪 
daily stress 日常压力 
not take seriously 不太当真 
Sample answer: 
I think dreams sometimes reflect emotions or daily stress rather than having special meanings. When I’m tired 
or worried, my dreams tend to be more intense or strange. Most of the time, though, I don’t take them too 
seriously and just see them as part of the brain resting. 
Question 4 
Do you want to make your dreams come true? 
Useful phrases: 
stay motivated 保持动力 
take small steps 迈出小步 
long-term goals 长期目标 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I definitely want to make my dreams come true, because having goals gives my life direction and meaning. 
I try to stay motivated by taking small steps every day instead of rushing or feeling pressured. Even if it takes 
time, working toward long-term goals makes me feel hopeful and confident. 
 
 

=== PAGE 6 ===
 
 
6 
 
 
Keys 
Question 1: 
Do you always bring a lot of keys with you? 
Useful phrases: 
keychain 钥匙串 
travel light 轻装出行 
feel secure 感到安心 
Sample answer: 
No, I don’t like carrying a lot of keys with me, because it feels heavy and inconvenient. I usually keep only the 
keys I really need on a small keychain so I can travel light. That way I still feel secure without carrying 
unnecessary things. 
Question 2: 
Have you ever lost your keys? 
Useful phrases: 
feel stressed 感到紧张 
search everywhere 到处找 
learn a lesson 吸取教训 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I have lost my keys before, and it was quite stressful at the time. I had to search everywhere and even 
thought about changing the lock. That experience helped me learn a lesson, and now I always check my bag 
before going out. 
Question 3 
Do you often forget the keys and lock yourself out? 
Useful phrases: 
be forgetful 健忘 
double-check 检查两遍 
learn a habit 养成习惯 
Sample answer: 
No, I don’t often lock myself out, because I’m careful with my keys. I used to be a bit forgetful, so now I always 
double-check before closing the door. That experience helped me learn a habit of keeping things organized. 
Question 4 
Do you think it’s a good idea to leave your keys with a neighbour? 
Useful phrases: 
trust someone 信任他人 
emergency situation 紧急情况 
feel safer 感到更安心 
Sample answer: 
I think it can be a good idea to leave keys with a neighbour if you trust someone and know them well. It’s 
especially helpful in an emergency situation, like locking yourself out. Personally, it makes me feel safer 
knowing there’s a backup option nearby. 
 
 

=== PAGE 7 ===
 
 
7 
 
 
Sports team 
Question 1: 
Have you ever been part of a sports team? 
Useful phrases: 
school team 校队 
team spirit 团队精神 
work together 合作 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I was once part of a school basketball team when I was younger. Being in a team taught me about team 
spirit and how to work together toward the same goal. Even though it was tiring, the experience was fun and 
memorable. 
Question 2: 
Are team sports popular in your culture? 
Useful phrases: 
be quite popular in my culture 在我的文化中很受欢迎 
learn how to work with others 学会如何与他人合作 
during big matches 在大型比赛期间 
Sample answer: 
Yes, team sports are quite popular in my culture. Many students play basketball, football, or volleyball at 
school. These activities help them stay healthy and learn how to work with others. I remember we often played 
in teams during PE classes, and it was a lot of fun. Watching team sports on TV is also common, especially 
during big matches. 
Question 3 
Do you like watching team games? Why? 
 
Useful phrases: 
full of energy and excitement 充满活力和刺激 
great teamwork and quick moves 出色的团队合作和快速动作 
cheering for the same team 为同一个队伍加油 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I do enjoy watching team games. The reason is that they are full of energy and excitement. I especially like 
football matches because you can see great teamwork and quick moves. I also enjoy watching with friends—it 
makes the experience even better. The feeling of cheering for the same team is really fun. 
Question 4 
What are the differences between team sports and individual sports? 
Useful phrases: 
a group of players working together 一组队员合作 
focus on one person’s performance 关注个人表现 
need strong self-motivation 需要很强的自我激励 
Sample answer: 
Team sports involve a group of players working together to achieve a goal, like winning a football or basketball 
match. Individual sports, such as tennis or running, focus on one person’s performance. The biggest difference 
is that team sports require good communication and cooperation, while individual sports need strong self-
motivation. I think both types can be fun, but they give people different kinds of challenges. 
 
 

=== PAGE 8 ===
 
 
8 
 
 
Pets and Animals 
Question 1: 
What’s your favorite animal? Why? 
Useful phrases: 
loyal nature 忠诚的天性 
friendly personality 友好的性格 
keep company 陪伴 
Sample answer: 
My favorite animal is the dog, mainly because of its loyal nature and friendly personality. Dogs are always 
excited to see their owners and can really keep company when people feel lonely. I think they make great 
companions for both families and individuals. 
Question 2: 
Where do you prefer to keep your pet, indoors or outdoors? 
Useful phrases: 
stay indoors 待在室内 
feel safe 感到安全 
spend time together 共度时间 
Sample answer: 
I prefer to keep my pet indoors, because it feels safer and more comfortable. That way I can spend time 
together with it and take better care of its health. I think pets are part of the family, so staying indoors makes 
more sense to me. 
Question 3 
Have you ever had a pet before? 
Useful phrases: 
take care of 照顾 
keep company 陪伴 
childhood memory 童年回忆 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I had a pet when I was younger, and it was a great experience. Taking care of it taught me responsibility, 
and it always kept me company after school. It’s one of my favorite childhood memories. 
Question 4 
What is the most popular animal in China? 
Useful phrases: 
national symbol 国家象征 
cultural meaning 文化含义 
loved by children 深受孩子喜爱 
Sample answer: 
I think the most popular animal in China is the panda, because it’s a national symbol with strong cultural 
meaning. Pandas are gentle, cute, and loved by children as well as adults. They also represent friendship and 
peace, which makes them especially meaningful to many people. 
 
 

=== PAGE 9 ===
 
 
9 
 
 
Food 
Question 1: 
What’s your favorite food? 
Useful phrases: 
comfort food 治愈系食物 
rich flavour 味道浓郁 
remind me of home 让我想到家 
Sample answer: 
My favorite food is dumplings, because they are a kind of comfort food for me. They have a rich flavour and can 
be made with many different fillings. More importantly, they remind me of home and family gatherings. 
Question 2: 
What kind of food did you like when you were young? 
Useful phrases: 
sweet snacks 甜味零食 
home-cooked meals 家常菜 
simple flavours 简单口味 
Sample answer: 
When I was young, I really liked sweet snacks such as candies and chocolate, because they always made me 
happy. At the same time, I enjoyed home-cooked meals prepared by my parents, especially dishes with simple 
flavours. Looking back, those foods were not only tasty but also connected with warm family memories. 
Question 3 
Do you eat different foods at different times of the year? 
Useful phrases: 
seasonal food 时令食物 
feel warmer 感到更暖和 
light meals 清淡饮食 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I do eat different foods at different times of the year, mainly because my body needs to change with the 
weather. In winter, I prefer hot dishes and soups that make me feel warmer, while in summer I usually choose 
seasonal food and light meals. Eating this way feels more comfortable and also helps me stay healthy 
throughout the year. 
Question 4 
Has your favorite food changed since you were a child? 
Useful phrases: 
eating habits 饮食习惯 
care about health 关注健康 
rich flavours 丰富口味 
Sample answer: 
Yes, my favorite food has changed quite a lot since I was a child. When I was younger, I preferred sweet snacks 
and fast food, but as my eating habits changed, I started to care about health and balance. Now I enjoy dishes 
with rich flavours but less oil, because they make me feel better both physically and mentally. 
 
 

=== PAGE 10 ===
 
 
10 
 
 
Day off 
Question 1: 
When was the last time you had a few days off? 
Useful phrases: 
short break 短暂假期 
relax my mind 放松大脑 
recharge energy 补充精力 
Sample answer: 
The last time I had a few days off was during a short holiday a few months ago. I didn’t travel far but stayed at 
home to relax my mind and sleep more. That break really helped me recharge energy and return to work 
refreshed. 
Question 2: 
What do you usually do when you have days off? 
Useful phrases: 
relax at home 在家放松 
catch up on sleep 补觉 
meet friends 见朋友 
Sample answer: 
When I have days off, I usually relax at home and catch up on sleep. Sometimes I meet friends for a meal or a 
short walk outside. These simple activities help me feel refreshed and ready for the next busy week. 
Question 3 
Do you usually spend your days off with your parents or with your friends? 
Useful phrases: 
quality time 共度时光 
relax together 一起放松 
depends on 情况而定 
Sample answer: 
It really depends on the situation, but I usually spend days off with my parents. We like to relax together, have 
meals, or just talk at home. I spend time with friends too, but family time feels more comfortable. 
Question 4 
What would you like to do if you had a day off tomorrow? 
Useful phrases: 
slow down 放慢节奏 
relax at home 在家放松 
enjoy personal time 享受个人时间 
Sample answer: 
If I had a day off tomorrow, I’d like to slow down and relax at home. I would probably sleep a bit more, watch 
something I enjoy, and maybe go for a short walk nearby. Having a quiet day helps me enjoy personal time and 
reset my energy. 
 
 

=== PAGE 11 ===
 
 
11 
 
 
Morning time 
Question 1: 
Do you like getting up early in the morning? 
Useful phrases: 
early riser 早起的人 
feel refreshed 感到清醒 
need enough sleep 需要充足睡眠 
Sample answer: 
I wouldn’t say I love getting up early, but I don’t hate it either. When I get enough sleep, waking up early 
actually makes me feel refreshed and productive. However, without enough rest, mornings can be quite painful 
for me. 
Question 2: 
What do you usually do in the morning? 
Useful phrases: 
get ready 准备出门 
check my phone 看手机 
start the day 开始一天 
Sample answer: 
In the morning, I usually get ready first and then check my phone for messages or updates. After that, I have a 
simple breakfast before leaving home. This routine helps me start the day calmly without feeling rushed. 
Question 3 
What did you do in the morning when you were little? Why? 
Useful phrases: 
a simple morning routine 一个简单的早晨习惯 
watching cartoons while eating 一边吃饭一边看动画 
keep good habits 保持良好的习惯 
Sample answer: 
When I was little, I usually had a simple morning routine. I woke up early, brushed my teeth, and had breakfast 
with my family. One thing I clearly remember is watching cartoons while eating. It was my favorite part of the 
day, mainly because it made mornings fun and helped me feel more awake. Sometimes, I also played with my 
toys for a short time before going to school. My parents wanted me to keep good habits, so mornings were 
always busy but enjoyable. 
Question 4 
Are there any differences between what you do in the morning now and what you did in the past? 
Useful phrases: 
used to get up late 过去常常晚起 
check my schedule for the day 查看我一天的日程 
help me feel more organized 让我更有条理 
Sample answer: 
Yes, there are some differences. When I was younger, I used to get up late and rush to school without much 
planning. But now I usually wake up earlier, make a cup of coffee, and check my schedule for the day. I’ve also 
developed a habit of doing some light stretching or listening to the news in the morning. These changes help 
me feel more organized and relaxed.

12 
 
 
Gifts 
Question 1: 
Have you ever sent handmade gifts to others? 
Useful phrases: 
handmade card 手工卡片 
show effort 表达用心 
special meaning 特殊意义 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I’ve sent handmade gifts like cards or small crafts to friends before. They may not look perfect, but they 
really show effort and care. I think handmade gifts have special meaning because they take time and thought. 
Question 2: 
Have you ever received a great gift? 
Useful phrases: 
meaningful gift 有意义的礼物 
show care 表达关心 
remember clearly 记得很清楚 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I once received a very meaningful gift from a close friend on my birthday. It wasn’t expensive, but it really 
showed care and thought. I still remember it clearly because it made me feel valued and appreciated. 
Question 3 
What do you consider when choosing a gift? 
Useful phrases: 
personal taste 个人喜好 
practical use 实用性 
show care 表达心意 
Sample answer: 
When choosing a gift, I first think about the person’s personal taste. I also consider whether the gift has 
practical use in daily life. Most importantly, I want it to show care rather than be expensive. 
Question 4 
Do you think you are good at choosing gifts? 
Useful phrases: 
pay attention to 关注 
personal preferences 个人喜好 
thoughtful choice 用心的选择 
Sample answer: 
I think I’m quite good at choosing gifts, because I usually pay attention to what people like in daily 
conversations. I try to consider their personal preferences instead of buying something expensive. For me, a 
thoughtful choice is more important than the price.

13 
 
 
Hobby 
Question 1: 
Do you have any hobbies? 
Useful phrases: 
in my free time 空闲时间 
relax myself 放松自己 
develop skills 提升技能 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I have a few hobbies that I enjoy in my free time, such as reading and light exercise. These activities help 
me relax myself after a busy day. I also feel they help me develop skills and keep a balanced lifestyle. 
Question 2: 
Did you have any hobbies when you were a child? 
Useful phrases: 
spend hours 花很多时间 
simple fun 简单的快乐 
childhood memory 童年回忆 
Sample answer: 
Yes, when I was a child, I had several hobbies like drawing and playing outside. I could spend hours doing these 
simple things without getting bored. Looking back, they are some of my favorite childhood memories. 
Question 3 
Do you have a hobby that you’ve had since childhood? 
Useful phrases: 
stick with 坚持 
relax my mind 放松心情 
long-term interest 长期兴趣 
Sample answer: 
Yes, reading has been a hobby of mine since childhood. I stuck with it because it helps me relax my mind and 
learn new things. Over time, it became a long-term interest rather than just a habit. 
Question 4 
Do you have the same hobbies as your family members? 
Useful phrases: 
share interests 共同兴趣 
spend time together 共度时间 
different tastes 不同喜好 
Sample answer: 
I share some hobbies with my family members, like watching movies or going for walks together. These shared 
interests help us spend time together and relax. However, we also have different tastes, which gives everyone 
their own personal space. 
 
 

=== PAGE 14 ===
 
 
14 
 
 
Reading 
Question 1: 
Do you like reading? 
Useful phrases: 
escape reality 逃离现实 
learn new ideas 学习新想法 
quiet time 安静时光 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I like reading, especially when I want some quiet time alone. Reading helps me escape reality for a while 
and enter different worlds. At the same time, I can learn new ideas without feeling stressed. 
Question 2: 
Do you prefer to read on paper or on a screen? 
Useful phrases: 
paper books 纸质书 
eye strain 眼睛疲劳 
digital convenience 数字便利 
Sample answer: 
I prefer reading on paper because it causes less eye strain and feels more relaxing. Paper books also help me 
focus better without notifications. Although screens are convenient, I still enjoy the feeling of turning real 
pages. 
Question 3 
When do you need to read carefully, and when not? 
Useful phrases: 
important information 重要信息 
skim through 快速浏览 
avoid mistakes 避免错误 
Sample answer: 
I read carefully when the information is important, like instructions or exam questions. In contrast, I usually 
skim through news or social media posts. Reading carefully helps me avoid mistakes, while skimming saves 
time. 
Question 4 
Do you prefer scanning or detailed reading? 
Useful phrases: 
prefer detailed reading 更喜欢精读 
read carefully 仔细阅读 
looking for something specific 寻找特定信息 
Sample answer: 
I usually prefer detailed reading because I like to understand everything clearly. When I read carefully, I can find 
useful facts and remember them longer. Although scanning is faster, I only use it when I’m looking for 
something specific, like a name or a number in a text. 
 
 

=== PAGE 15 ===
 
 
15 
 
 
Walking 
Question 1: 
Do you walk a lot? 
Useful phrases: 
daily routine 日常习惯 
stay active 保持活动 
short distances 短距离 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I walk quite a lot as part of my daily routine, especially for short distances. Walking helps me stay active 
without needing special equipment. It’s also a good way to relax and clear my mind. 
Question 2: 
Did you often go outside to have a walk when you were a child? 
Useful phrases: 
play outdoors 户外玩耍 
fresh air 新鲜空气 
after school 放学后 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I often went outside to walk or play after school when I was a child. My parents encouraged me to get 
fresh air instead of staying indoors all the time. Those outdoor moments made my childhood more active and 
fun. 
Question 3 
Why do people like to walk in parks? 
Useful phrases: 
fresh air 新鲜空气 
natural environment 自然环境 
reduce stress 缓解压力 
Sample answer: 
People like walking in parks because they can enjoy fresh air and a natural environment. It’s a simple way to 
reduce stress and escape busy city life. Walking there also feels relaxing and refreshing. 
Question 4 
Where would you like to take a long walk if you had the chance? 
Useful phrases: 
seaside path 海边小路 
peaceful atmosphere 宁静的氛围 
clear my mind 清理思绪 
Sample answer: 
If I had the chance, I’d love to take a long walk along a seaside path. The peaceful atmosphere and sound of 
waves would help me relax and clear my mind. Walking there slowly would be a perfect way to escape stress 
and enjoy nature. 
 
 

=== PAGE 16 ===
 
 
16 
 
 
Typing 
Question 1: 
Do you prefer typing or handwriting? 
Useful phrases: 
it’s faster and more convenient 更快也更方便 
easily delete or change things 轻松删除或更改内容 
for everyday tasks, typing works better 对于日常任务来说，打字更合适 
Sample answer: 
I prefer typing, mainly because it’s faster and more convenient. When I’m writing on my laptop, I can easily 
delete or change things without making a mess. Also, I often use typing for emails and homework. Handwriting 
is nice sometimes, like when I want to write a birthday card, but for everyday tasks, typing works better for me. 
Question 2: 
Do you type on a desktop or laptop keyboard everyday? 
Useful phrases: 
work tasks 工作任务 
typing speed 打字速度 
daily habit 日常习惯 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I type on a laptop keyboard almost every day because most of my work tasks are done on a computer. 
Over time, this has improved my typing speed without me noticing. Using a keyboard has become a daily habit 
for me. 
Question 3 
When did you learn how to type on a keyboard? 
Useful phrases: 
learn how to type 学会打字 
make mistakes 出错 
finish my work efficiently 高效完成工作 
Sample answer: 
I learned how to type on a keyboard when I was in primary school, mainly because we had computer classes 
every week. At first, I made many mistakes, but with practice, I became quite fast. Now I can type quickly 
without looking at the keys, which helps me finish my work more efficiently. 
Question 4 
How do you improve your typing? 
Useful phrases: 
practice regularly 经常练习 
typing speed 打字速度 
daily use 日常使用 
Sample answer: 
I improve my typing mainly by practicing regularly through daily use. Writing emails, assignments, and 
messages naturally increases my typing speed. Over time, typing has become automatic without me focusing 
on it. 
 
 

=== PAGE 17 ===
 
 
17 
 
 
Building 
Question 1: 
Are there tall buildings near your home? 
Useful phrases: 
quite a few tall buildings 有不少高楼 
a busy city area 繁忙的城市区域 
make the city look more developed and lively 让城市看起来更现代、更有活力 
Sample answer: 
Yes, there are quite a few tall buildings near where I live. I live in a busy city area, so there are office buildings,

Plants 
Question 1: 
Do you keep plants at home? 
Useful phrases: 
I keep a few small plants at home. 我家里养了几盆小植物。 
They bring a lot of joy. 给我带来很多快乐。 
make the room look fresh 让房间看起来更清新 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I keep a few small plants at home, like a cactus and some green leafy ones. Taking care of them helps me 
relax, and I feel happy when I see them grow. Plants also make the room look fresh and more lively. I water 
them every few days and sometimes move them to get enough sunlight. They don’t need much care, but they 
bring a lot of joy to my daily life. 
Question 2: 
What plant did you grow when you were young? 
Useful phrases: 
I remember watering it. 我记得我给它浇水。 
make me feel proud 让我感到自豪 
learn about nature and responsibility 了解自然和责任感 
Sample answer: 
When I was young, I grew a small tomato plant on the balcony with my parents. I remember watering it every 
day and watching it grow taller and taller. It was exciting to see the tiny green tomatoes turn red. That 
experience made me feel proud and taught me patience. I think growing plants is a fun way to learn about 
nature and responsibility. 
Question 3 
Do you know anything about growing a plant? 
Useful phrases: 
watch them grow day by day 一天天看着它们长大 
make me feel peaceful 让我感到平静 
teach me patience 教会我耐心 
Sample answer: 
Yes, I’ve grown some plants at home before, like mint and small flowers. First, I learned that plants need 
sunlight, water, and good soil. I usually water them in the morning and check if the soil is dry. Watching them 
grow day by day makes me feel peaceful. Once, I even tried growing tomatoes, and I was so excited when I saw 
the first red one. Growing plants has taught me patience and how to take care of living things. 
Question 4 
Do Chinese people send plants as gifts? 
Useful phrases: 
housewarming or business openings 搬家或开业场合 
believed to bring good luck 被认为能带来好运 
a thoughtful gift 一份有心意的礼物 
Sample answer: 
Yes, Chinese people sometimes send plants as gifts, especially for housewarming or business openings. Plants 
like lucky bamboo or money trees are popular because they are believed to bring good luck and success. I’ve 
seen people give potted flowers too, especially during holidays like the Spring Festival. Sending plants shows 
care and hope for someone’s future. It’s a thoughtful gift that lasts longer than flowers. I think it’s a nice way to 
show good wishes.

Yes, I don’t mind lending things to others, especially if I trust my friends and know they will take good care of 
them. Sometimes I feel uncomfortable lending expensive items, but for books or small stuff it’s fine. Actually, 
lending things often makes our friendship stronger. 
Question 4 
How do you feel when people don’t return things they borrowed from you? 
Useful phrases: 
feel annoyed 感到恼火 
lose trust 失去信任 
small disappointment 小失望 
Sample answer: 
I usually feel annoyed when people don’t return the things they borrowed, even if the item isn’t very 
expensive. It makes me lose trust in them, because I expect friends to be responsible. Honestly, it’s a small 
disappointment that sometimes changes how I see the friendship.

Advertisement

unforgettable memory 难忘的记忆

Question 2: 
Do you see a lot of advertising on trains or other transport?

Yes, I see a lot of advertising on trains and buses, especially big eye-catching posters about food delivery or

Question 3 
Do you like advertisements?

creative ideas 有创意的想法

catch my attention 吸引我的注意 
Sample answer: 
I only like advertisements when they are creative and fun, because they can really catch my attention. But I get

ideas, but boring ones just waste time. 
Question 4

funny stories 搞笑故事 
positive message 积极的信息 
Sample answer: 
I like advertising that has creative design and makes me smile, like funny stories in short videos. Sometimes ads 
with a positive message also impress me, especially if they focus on family or friendship. I think these types of 
ads are more meaningful than just showing products.

Yes, I think museums are very important because they preserve history and show us things we can’t see in daily

museums can broaden horizons and make people appreciate the past more. 
Question 2: 
Are there many museums in your hometown?

educational trips 教育参观

No, my hometown doesn’t have many museums, maybe only a small one showing local culture and crafts. If I 
want to see more historical artifacts, I usually need to go to a bigger city nearby. Still, that small museum is

Question 3

more often.

exhibition on ancient history, and it was really interesting. I enjoyed the visit because I got to learn something 
new outside the classroom.

Having a break

I usually take a short break every hour when I’m studying, because it helps me recharge energy and stay 
focused. Sometimes I just stretch, grab some water, or check my phone for a few minutes. Taking breaks 
regularly keeps me more productive and less tired. 
Question 2: 
What do you usually do when you are resting? 
Useful phrases: 
listen to music 听音乐 
recharge myself 给自己充电 
scroll through my phone 刷手机 
Sample answer: 
When I’m resting, I usually listen to music or just scroll through my phone to relax. Sometimes I lie on the sofa

Question 3 
Do you take a nap when you are taking your rest?

Yes, I often take a short nap in the afternoon, usually for about twenty minutes. Even a quick rest can recharge

stay focused.

Sharing 
Question 1: 
Did your parents teach you to share when you were a child? 
Useful phrases: 
good manners 良好的礼貌 
share toys 分享玩具 
think of others 替别人着想 
Sample answer: 
Yes, my parents always taught me to share when I was little, especially with my cousins and classmates. They 
told me sharing toys and food was part of good manners, and it helped me make friends more easily. I think 
those lessons also taught me to think of others, not just myself, which I still find valuable today. 
Question 2: 
What kind of things do you like to share with others? 
Useful phrases: 
daily snacks 日常零食 
useful advice 有用的建议 
good memories 美好的回忆 
Sample answer: 
I usually like to share daily snacks with my friends, because eating together always makes the moment more 
fun. Sometimes I also share useful advice about studying or daily problems, since it feels nice to help others. 
More importantly, I enjoy sharing good memories, like old photos or funny stories, because they bring us 
closer. 
Question 3 
What kind of things are not suitable for sharing? 
Useful phrases: 
personal items 私人物品 
keep hygiene 保持卫生 
avoid problems 避免麻烦 
Sample answer: 
I think personal items like toothbrushes, towels, or cosmetics are not suitable for sharing because of hygiene 
issues. Money is also tricky to share, since it can easily cause arguments between friends. To avoid problems, I 
prefer to only share safe things like snacks or books. 
Question 4 
Do you have anything to share with others recently? 
Useful phrases: 
good news 好消息 
useful tips 实用建议 
daily snacks 日常零食 
Sample answer:

on study apps or learning methods.

Part 2&3 
【当季新题】2026 年01-04 月Part 2&3 正式题库和解析 
People【人】 
擅长做计划的人 
Describe a person who makes plans a lot and is good at planning 
You should say: 
Who he or she is 
How you knew him or her 
What plans he or she makes 
And explain how you feel about this person 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物类+性格习惯类”话题，重点在于描述一个非常爱做计划的人。需要回答四点：这个人是谁、你如
何认识他或她、他或她通常做什么样的计划、以及你对这个人的看法和感受。时态以现在时为主，介绍认识过程时
可用过去时。 
思路方面 
可以选择身边真实的人，比如同学、朋友、同事或家人。重点不是“计划多复杂”，而是计划的频率和习惯，例如
学习计划、时间安排、旅行计划、日常生活清单等。最后要表达你对这种性格的态度，可以是欣赏、学习，或既喜
欢又觉得有压力。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这个人是谁，以及你是如何认识他或她的； 
第二段：具体说明他或她常做哪些计划，以及表现出来的习惯； 
第三段：表达你对这个人的看法和感受，并进行总结。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
 
He is one of my closest friends. 他是我最亲近的朋友之一。 
I got to know him in high school. 我在高中认识他的。 
We have known each other for many years. 我们认识很多年了。 
She is the kind of person who likes order. 她是一个喜欢有条理的人。 
Planning is part of his daily life. 计划已经成为他日常生活的一部分。 
具体描述 
He makes study plans every week. 他每周都会制定学习计划。 
She writes down her tasks in a notebook. 她会把任务写在本子里。 
He plans trips in detail, including time and budget. 他会把旅行的时间和预算都计划好。 
She likes to prepare things in advance. 她喜欢提前准备事情。 
He rarely does things without a plan. 他几乎不做没有计划的事。 
描述感受 
I admire his self-discipline. 我很佩服他的自律。 
This habit makes him very reliable. 这个习惯让他非常可靠。 
Sometimes I feel pressured, but also motivated. 有时我有压力，但也被激励。 
I have learned to plan better from him. 我从他身上学会了更好地做计划。 
Overall, I respect this way of living. 总的来说，我很尊重这种生活方式。 
 
 
 

=== PAGE 37 ===
 
 
37 
 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A person who makes plans a lot is my close friend David. I got to know him in high school, and we have stayed 
in touch ever since. From the very beginning, I noticed that he was very different from most people around me, 
because he always liked to arrange things in advance. 
David makes plans for almost everything in his life. He has weekly study plans, daily to-do lists, and even plans 
for weekends. For example, before an exam week, he writes down what subject to study each day and how 
much time to spend on it. When we travel together, he plans the schedule, transport, and even meal times. He 
also keeps reminders on his phone and a small notebook to track his progress. Because of this habit, he rarely 
feels rushed or confused. 
I have mixed but mostly positive feelings about this person. On the one hand, I really admire his self-discipline 
and organization. He is very reliable, and I feel safe working with him on group tasks. On the other hand, his 
detailed planning sometimes makes me feel a little pressured, because I am more relaxed by nature. However, I 
have learned a lot from him, especially how planning can save time and reduce stress. Overall, I respect his way 
of living, and I believe this habit will help him succeed in the future. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Do you think it’s important to plan ahead? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“减少压力”“提高效率”“应对变化”来说明提前规划的重要性。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, planning ahead is important. When people make plans, they know what to do and feel less stressed. 
Planning helps them use time better and avoid mistakes. 
For example, planning study or work tasks helps people finish things on time. Planning also prepares people for 
possible problems. 
 
Question 2: What activities do we need to plan ahead? 
解题思路：说明与原因类问题。可以从“活动复杂度高”“涉及多人或资源”“时间和费用成本高”这几个角度
展开，解释为什么有些活动如果不提前计划就容易出问题。重点放在“提前规划能解决什么问题”。 
Sample Answer: 
Many activities need to be planned ahead, especially those that involve time, money, or other people. Traveling 
is a good example. People need to book tickets, hotels, and plan routes, or the trip may become stressful. 
Big events like weddings, parties, or meetings also need planning. Without preparation, things may go wrong, 
such as missing items or schedule problems. 
Even study plans and work projects benefit from planning. Planning ahead helps people use time better, reduce 
stress, and feel more confident. 
 
Question 3: Do you think children should plan their future career? 
解题思路：观点类问题。重点不是“定死职业”，而是解释“早期思考”的好处，并说明不应给孩子太大压力。 
Sample Answer: 
I think children can think about their future career, but they should not plan it too strictly. Early thinking helps 
children understand their interests and strengths. It can also motivate them to study better. 
However, children are still growing, and their interests may change. If parents push them too hard, children 
may feel stressed or lose confidence. 
So, it is good for children to explore different jobs, but career planning should be flexible and pressure-free. 
 
Question 4: Should children ask their teachers or parents for advice when making plans? 
解题思路：对比与观点类问题。可以从“父母与老师角色不同”入手，解释父母更了解孩子的性格和生活，而
老师更熟悉学习和发展路径。重点不是二选一，而是说明在不同情境下应向不同的人求助。 
Sample Answer: 
I think children should ask both teachers and parents for advice when making plans. Parents know their 
children very well. They understand their personality, habits, and daily life, so their advice is often caring and 
supportive. 
Teachers, on the other hand, have experience in education and planning for the future. They can give useful 
advice about study goals, skills, and learning paths. 
 
 

=== PAGE 38 ===
 
 
38 
 
 
喜欢画画的孩子 
Describe a child who loves drawing or painting 
You should say: 
Who he or she is 
How or when you knew him or her 
How often he or she draws or paints 
And explain why you think he or she loves drawing or painting 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物类 + 兴趣爱好类”话题，要求你描述一位非常喜欢画画或绘画的孩子。题目需要你说清：这个孩子
是谁、你是如何或在什么时候认识他或她的、他或她画画的频率，以及你为什么认为他或她真的热爱画画。整体以
现在时描述习惯，用过去时补充认识经过，重点在于持续行为和内在动机。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择你现实中接触过的孩子，比如朋友的孩子或社区里的小朋友。思路上可以先说清你是通过什么场合认
识这个孩子的；然后要说清他或她多久画一次画；接着可以重点说你观察到的细节，比如是否主动画画、是否专
注、是否从中获得快乐；最后总结你为什么觉得这是真正的热爱。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这个孩子是谁，以及你是如何或什么时候认识他或她的；第二段：描述他或她画画的频率、内容和日
常表现；第三段：解释你为什么认为他或她热爱画画，并表达你的感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The child is my friend’s son. 这个孩子是我朋友的儿子。 
I met him at a community center. 我是在社区活动中心认识他的。 
He is around seven years old. 他大约七岁。 
He is friendly and imaginative. 他很友好，也很有想象力。 
Drawing is his favorite activity. 画画是他最喜欢的活动。 
具体描述 
He draws almost every evening. 他几乎每天晚上都会画画。 
He likes using colored pencils. 他喜欢用彩铅。 
He often draws stories he imagines. 他经常画自己想象的故事。 
He can sit and draw for a long time. 他可以坐着画很久。 
He enjoys talking about his drawings. 他喜欢讲自己的画。 
描述感受 
Drawing helps him express ideas. 画画帮助他表达想法。 
It makes him feel relaxed and happy. 这让他感到放松和快乐。 
I can see his focus and patience. 我能看到他的专注和耐心。 
He draws for enjoyment, not results. 他画画是为了享受过程。 
That is why I believe he loves drawing. 这就是我认为他热爱画画的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A child who loves drawing is my friend’s son, who is about seven years old. I first met him last year at a 
community center where several families often gather on weekends. At that time, I noticed that while other 
children were running around, he was sitting quietly at a table with paper and pencils. That was how I first 
realized his strong interest in drawing. 
He draws almost every evening after finishing his homework. According to his parents, drawing has become 
part of his daily routine. He likes using colored pencils and often draws animals, cartoon characters, and small 
stories from his imagination.  
 
 

=== PAGE 39 ===
 
 
39 
 
 
Sometimes he draws scenes from his school life, such as his classroom or playground. What impressed me 
most is that he can stay focused for a long time. Even when the environment is noisy, he keeps drawing 
patiently and rarely gets distracted. After finishing a picture, he enjoys explaining the story behind it to people 
around him. 
I think he truly loves drawing because it helps him express ideas in a natural way. He is not a child who talks a 
lot, but through drawing, he can clearly show what he is thinking about. Drawing also makes him feel calm and 
confident. He does not draw because someone asks him to, but because he enjoys the process itself. Watching 
him draw always makes me feel relaxed, because I can see how happy and focused he is. That is why I believe 
drawing is not just a hobby for him, but something he genuinely loves doing every day. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: What is the right age for a child to learn drawing? 
解题思路：观点 + 原因类问题。重点不是给“唯一年龄”，而是解释为什么幼儿阶段适合开始。 
Sample Answer: 
I think children can start learning drawing at a young age, around four or five. At this age, children enjoy colors 
and shapes and like to express ideas freely. 
Drawing helps them develop creativity and hand skills. It should be fun, not stressful. There is no need for strict 
rules at first. 
So, early drawing is good as long as it is relaxed and enjoyable. 
 
Question 2: Why do most children draw more often than adults do? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“时间”“压力”“表达方式”解释为什么儿童更常画画。 
Sample Answer: 
Most children draw more often because they have more free time and fewer worries. Drawing is a natural way 
for children to express ideas and feelings. They enjoy using colors and imagination without thinking too much 
about results. 
Adults are usually busy with work and family, so they have less time. They may also feel shy or think they are 
not good at drawing. 
So, children draw more because drawing feels easy, fun, and stress-free for them. 
 
Question 3: Why do some people visit galleries or museums instead of viewing artworks online? 
解题思路：原因类问题。重点解释“现场体验”的价值，并对比线上观看的局限。 
Sample Answer: 
Some people visit galleries or museums because they want a real experience. Seeing artworks in person helps 
people feel the size, color, and details better. 
Museums also offer a quiet and special environment, which helps people focus and learn. Online viewing is 
convenient, but it cannot replace the feeling of being there. 
So, people visit museums to enjoy art more deeply and seriously. 
 
Question 4: Do you think galleries and museums should be free of charge? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以采取“部分免费或低价”的平衡立场，解释文化公平与运营成本之间的关系。 
Sample Answer: 
I think galleries and museums should be free or low-cost. Free entry allows more people, especially children 
and low-income families, to learn about culture and history. It helps education and social equality. 
However, museums need money to protect artworks and run programs. Without income, quality may drop. 
So, free entry on certain days or lower prices are a good balance between access and management. 
 
 

=== PAGE 40 ===
 
 
40 
 
 
想见的名人 
Describe a famous person you would like to meet 
You should say: 
Who he or she is 
How you knew him or her 
How or where you would like to meet him or her 
And explain why you would like to meet him or her 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物类 + 个人愿望类”话题，要求你描述一位你想见面的名人。需要说明：他或她是谁、你是如何认识
或了解到他或她的、你希望在什么场合或地点见面，以及你为什么想见他或她。整体以现在时和将来时为主，介绍
认识过程时可用过去时。重点在于个人原因和情感动机。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择歌手、演员、运动员或作家。思路上可以先说清这个人是谁，以及你最早是通过什么方式知道他的；
然后可以说一说你希望在哪里、以什么方式见到他；最后可以重点说你想见他的原因，比如受到启发、喜欢他的作
品或性格。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这位名人是谁，以及你是如何认识他的； 
第二段：说明你希望在什么地方、什么情境下见到他； 
第三段：解释你为什么想见他，并总结你的感受。 
 
答题参考 
 
He is a famous singer in my country. 他是我国家非常有名的歌手。 
I first knew him through his songs. 我最早是通过他的歌曲认识他的。 
He has been popular for many years. 他已经红了很多年。 
Many people of my age grew up listening to him. 很多和我同龄的人都是听着他的歌长大的。 
He is well known for his talent and style. 他因才华和风格而出名 
具体描述 
I would like to meet him at a music event. 我希望在音乐活动上见到他。 
It would be great to talk with him face to face. 如果能面对面交流会很棒。 
I want to tell him how his work influenced me. 我想告诉他他的作品对我的影响。 
I imagine the meeting would be short but meaningful. 我想象这次见面会很短但很有意义。 
I would feel nervous but excited. 我会既紧张又兴奋。 
描述感受 
I admire his creativity and hard work. 我钦佩他的创造力和努力。 
He inspired me during my teenage years. 他在我青少年时期给了我启发。 
Meeting him would be a dream come true. 见到他将是梦想成真。 
I believe the experience would motivate me. 我相信这次经历会激励我。 
That is why I really want to meet him. 这就是我很想见他的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A famous person I would really like to meet is Jay Chou. He is a very well-known singer and songwriter in the 
Chinese-speaking world. I first knew him when I was in primary school, because many of my classmates 
listened to his songs, and his music was often played on the radio and TV. 
I would like to meet him at a music event or a small concert if possible. I imagine meeting him backstage after a 
performance would be ideal. I don’t expect to have a long conversation, but I would love to talk with him face 
to face for a few minutes. 

=== PAGE 41 ===
 
 
41 
 
 
 I want to tell him how much his songs meant to me while growing up and how they helped me relax during 
stressful times. I think I would feel nervous at first, but also very excited and grateful for the chance. 
I want to meet Jay Chou because I truly admire his creativity and dedication to music. He combines modern 
music with traditional Chinese elements, which makes his work special and meaningful. His songs accompanied 
me during my teenage years and left many strong memories. Meeting him would feel like meeting someone 
who shaped part of my youth. That is why I really hope to meet him one day, even if it is just for a short 
moment. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: What are the advantages and disadvantages of being a famous child? 
解题思路：评估类问题。需要同时解释好处和问题。 
Sample Answer: 
Being a famous child has advantages. They get more chances, money, and attention. They may start a career 
early. 
But there are disadvantages too. Famous children have less privacy and more pressure. They may lose a normal 
childhood. 
So, fame brings opportunities, but it also brings stress and responsibility. 
 
Question 2: What can today’s children do to become famous? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从网络平台、才艺展示、内容创作展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Today’s children can become famous through the internet. They can share talents like singing, drawing, or 
sports online. Social media gives them a large audience. 
Some also join talent shows or competitions. However, fame should not be the main goal. Children still need 
education and guidance. 
So, technology offers chances, but fame should come naturally and safely. 
 
Question 3: What can children do with their fame? 
解题思路：说明 + 评估类问题。可以说明积极用途，同时提醒风险。 
Sample Answer: 
Children can use fame to share positive messages and inspire others. They may support good causes or show 
their talents. 
However, fame also brings pressure. Children need guidance to handle attention and protect privacy. 
So, fame can be useful, but children need support to use it wisely. 
 
Question 4: Do people become famous because of their talent? 
解题思路：原因 + 评估类问题。可以说明“天赋重要但不唯一”。 
Sample Answer: 
Talent helps people become famous, but it is not the only reason. People with strong skills in music, sports, or 
acting often get attention. 
However, luck, timing, and social media also matter. Some talented people are not famous, while others gain 
fame quickly online. 
So, talent is important, but success depends on many factors.

鼓励你保护自然的人 
Describe a person who encouraged you to protect the nature 
You should say: 
Who he or she is 
How he or she encouraged you 
What he or she encouraged you to do 
And explain how you feel about this person 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物类 + 环保意识类”话题，要求你描述一位鼓励你保护自然的人。需要说明：他或她是谁、他或她是
如何鼓励你的、具体鼓励你做了什么，以及你对这个人的感受。整体以过去时叙述经历，用现在时总结影响和感
受。重点在于影响方式和个人改变。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择老师、家人或朋友。思路上可以先说清这个人是谁以及你们的关系；然后可以说一说他或她通过哪些
方式鼓励你，比如言语、行动或活动；接着重点可以放在他或她具体让你做了哪些环保行为；最后说明你对这个人
的态度以及这件事对你的长期影响。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这个人是谁，以及你是如何认识他的； 
第二段：描述他或她如何鼓励你，并让你做了哪些事情； 
第三段：解释你对这个人的感受，以及这次经历的意义。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The person is my biology teacher. 这个人是我的生物老师。 
I met him during high school. 我是在高中认识他的。 
He cares deeply about the environment. 他非常关心环境。 
He often talked about nature in class. 他经常在课堂上谈到自然。 
He influenced me in a positive way. 他对我产生了积极影响。 
具体描述 
He encouraged us to reduce waste. 他鼓励我们减少浪费。 
He asked us to use reusable items. 他让我们使用可重复使用的物品。 
He organized a clean-up activity. 他组织了一次清理活动。 
He led by example. 他以身作则。 
He explained why small actions matter. 他解释了小行动的重要性。 
描述感受 
I feel grateful for his guidance. 我很感激他的引导。 
He changed the way I think about nature. 他改变了我对自然的看法。 
I respect him a lot. 我非常尊敬他。 
His words still influence me today. 他的话至今仍影响着我。 
That is why he means a lot to me. 这就是他对我很重要的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A person who encouraged me to protect nature is my biology teacher from high school. I met him when I was 
around sixteen years old, and he left a strong impression on me because he truly cared about the environment. 
He did not only teach from textbooks, but also shared his own actions and ideas. 
He encouraged me by explaining environmental problems in a simple and clear way. In class, he often talked 
about pollution, waste, and climate change, and he helped us understand how daily habits can affect nature. 
He encouraged us to reduce waste, use reusable bags and bottles, and save water and electricity at home. He 
also organized a clean-up activity in a nearby park, where we picked up rubbish together. By taking part in this 

=== PAGE 43 ===
 
 
43 
 
 
activity, I realized that protecting nature does not always require big actions. Small efforts can also make a 
difference. 
I feel grateful and respectful toward this teacher. He encouraged me patiently and never forced his ideas on us. 
Because of him, I started paying more attention to my behavior and became more responsible toward the 
environment. Even now, I still remember his words and try to live in a more eco-friendly way. He changed the 
way I think about nature, and that is why I truly admire and appreciate him. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: How can parents teach their children to protect nature? 
解题思路：解决方式类问题。可以从“以身作则”“日常小行为”“亲身体验”三个角度展开，重点解释父母如
何通过生活中的具体做法影响孩子，而不是只停留在说教层面。 
Sample Answer: 
Parents can teach children to protect nature by setting a good example. When children see parents saving 
water, sorting rubbish, or using fewer plastic bags, they learn naturally. 
Parents can also explain simple ideas, such as why trees are important or why animals need protection. Taking 
children to parks or nature areas helps them feel close to the environment. 
Small actions, like not wasting food and keeping places clean, make children understand responsibility. 
So, through daily habits, clear explanations, and real experiences, parents can help children care about nature. 
 
Question 2: Should schools teach children to get close to nature? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“身心发展”“环境意识”“学习方式多样化”三个角度展开，解释学校为什么
有责任引导孩子亲近自然，而不仅是完成课堂教学。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think schools should teach children to get close to nature. Nature helps children relax and stay healthy, 
especially when they spend a lot of time indoors. Being outside can reduce stress and improve mood. 
Schools can also use nature to teach students about the environment. When children see plants, animals, and 
natural spaces, they understand why protection is important. Learning outside makes lessons more interesting 
and real. 
So, helping children get close to nature supports both their health and their learning. 
 
Question 3: Do you think there should be laws to protect nature? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“个人行为不够”“法律约束力强”“保护公共利益”三个角度展开，解释为什
么仅靠自觉不够，需要法律来规范行为并长期保护自然环境。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think there should be laws to protect nature. Not everyone chooses to protect the environment by 
themselves, especially when it costs time or money. Laws can guide people to act responsibly. 
For example, rules about pollution, waste, and wildlife protection help reduce damage to nature. Laws also 
make companies more careful about how they use natural resources. 
So, laws are important because they protect nature in a fair and long-term way, not just by personal choice.

机智解决问题的人 
Describe a person who solved a problem in a smart way 
You should say: 
Who this person is 
What the problem was 
How he or she solved it 
And explain why you think he or she did it in a smart way 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物类 + 问题解决类”话题，要求你描述一位用聪明方式解决问题的人。需要说明：这个人是谁、遇到
了什么问题、他或她是如何解决的，以及你为什么认为这种方式很聪明。整体以过去时叙述事件，用现在时总结评
价。重点在于解决思路本身，而不是问题有多复杂。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择同学、同事或家人。思路上可以先说清这个人的身份和你们的关系；然后要说清当时遇到的具体问
题；接着可以重点说他或她采取了哪些步骤来解决问题；最后说明你觉得这种方法聪明的原因，比如冷静、有效或
节省时间。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这个人是谁，以及事情发生的背景； 
第二段：描述问题是什么，以及他或她是如何解决的； 
第三段：解释你为什么认为这是一个聪明的解决方式，并总结你的感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The person is my classmate. 这个人是我的同学。 
I have known him for several years. 我认识他好几年了。 
The situation happened during a group project. 事情发生在一次小组项目中。 
We were under a lot of pressure. 我们当时压力很大。 
Time was very limited. 时间非常紧。 
具体描述 
There was a serious problem with our plan. 我们的计划出现了严重问题。 
He stayed calm instead of panicking. 他保持冷静，没有慌乱。 
He broke the problem into smaller parts. 他把问题拆分成小部分。 
He suggested a simple and practical solution. 他提出了一个简单又实用的解决办法。 
Everyone agreed to follow his idea. 大家都同意按照他的想法来做。 
描述感受 
I was impressed by his way of thinking. 我对他的思路印象很深。 
His solution saved us a lot of time. 他的办法帮我们节省了很多时间。 
It showed his clear thinking. 这体现了他清晰的思维。 
I learned how to deal with problems calmly. 我学到了要冷静地处理问题。 
That is why I think he solved it in a smart way. 这就是我认为他解决得很聪明的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A person who solved a problem in a smart way is my classmate, whom I have known for several years. The 
situation happened during a group project at school, when we were working under a lot of pressure and had 
very little time left. Everyone felt nervous because the project was important for our final grade. 
The problem was that our original plan did not work. We realized that some information we prepared was 
wrong, and we did not have enough time to start everything again. While most of us were worried and did not 
know what to do, my classmate stayed calm. He suggested that we stop for a few minutes and look at the 
problem carefully. He broke the task into smaller parts and found which parts could still be used.  

=== PAGE 45 ===
 
 
45 
 
 
Then he suggested changing the structure of the project instead of replacing all the content. This helped us 
keep the key ideas and save time. Everyone agreed with his idea and followed his plan. 
I think he solved the problem in a smart way because he did not panic. He thought clearly and focused on what 
was possible instead of what went wrong. His solution was simple, practical, and effective. It helped the whole 
group finish the project on time and get a good result. I was really impressed by his way of thinking, and I 
learned that staying calm and organized is very important when facing problems. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Do you think children are born smart or they learn to become smart? 
解题思路：观点 + 对比类问题。可以采用“先天 + 后天结合”的思路，解释天赋的作用，同时重点说明学习和
环境对智力发展的重要性。 
Sample Answer: 
I think children are born with different abilities, but learning is more important in becoming smart. Some 
children may learn faster at first, but effort and education shape intelligence over time. 
Good teaching, reading habits, and practice help children develop thinking skills. Family support and learning 
environment also play a big role. 
Even children who are not very strong at the beginning can become smart through learning and hard work. 
So, being smart is not only about birth, but mostly about learning and experience. 
 
Question 2: How do children become smart at school? 
解题思路：原因与过程类问题。可以从“课堂学习”“练习与思考”“老师引导”和“学习态度”来解释孩子在
学校如何逐步变得更聪明。 
Sample Answer: 
Children become smart at school through learning and practice. Teachers explain knowledge and help students 
understand new ideas step by step. Asking questions and thinking in class also improve learning ability. 
Doing homework and reading help children remember and use what they learn. Group work and discussions 
teach them how to think and solve problems. 
Most importantly, a positive attitude makes a big difference. When children are curious and willing to learn, 
they become smarter over time. 
 
Question 3: Why are some people well-rounded and others only good at one thing? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“兴趣范围”“成长环境”“个人选择”三个方面解释差异，说明这是长期学习
和生活方式不同造成的结果，而不是对错问题。 
Sample Answer: 
Some people are well-rounded because they try many different activities when growing up. They enjoy 
learning new skills and exploring different interests. Family support and school experience also help them 
develop in many areas. 
Others focus on one thing because they find something they truly love and spend most of their time on it. This 
helps them become very skilled in one area. 
So, people develop differently because of interests, choices, and opportunities in life. 
 
Question 4: Why does modern society need talents of all kinds? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“社会分工复杂化”“不同领域相互配合”“问题多样化”三个角度展开，重点
解释为什么单一能力无法满足现代社会的需要，因此需要多种类型的人才共同合作。 
Sample Answer: 
Modern society needs talents of all kinds because life and work are more complex than before. Different jobs 
require different skills, such as technology, education, health care, and art. No single person can do everything 
well. 
Talents from different fields work together to solve problems. For example, engineers build systems, teachers 
train people, and doctors protect health. Each role is important. 
People also have different strengths and interests. When everyone uses their own talent, society runs more 
smoothly and creatively. 
So, modern society needs many kinds of talents to grow and develop in a balanced way.

乐于助人的人 
Describe a person who often helps others 
You should say: 
Who this person is 
How often he or she helps others 
How/why he or she helps others 
And how you feel about this person 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物 + 品质类”题目，重点在于描述一位经常帮助他人的人。题目不仅要求你说明这个人是谁，还要交
代他或她帮助他人的频率、方式和动机，最后补充你对这个人的情感态度。整体时态以一般现在时为主，必要时可
以回顾过去的具体例子。 
思路方面 
你可以选择身边真实存在的人，比如同学、同事、邻居或家人。重点不在于他或她做了多么“伟大”的事情，而在
于长期、持续的帮助行为。帮助的形式可以很日常，例如解答问题、提供情绪支持或主动照顾他人。在原因部分，
可以强调性格、价值观或成长经历。 
结构方面 
第一段介绍这个人的身份以及你与他或她的关系。 
第二段重点描述他或她通常如何、多久帮助别人，以及背后的原因。 
第三段表达你对这个人的感受，以及这种行为对你产生的影响。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
He is a close friend of mine. 他是我的一位好朋友。 
I’ve known him for many years. 我认识他已经很多年了。 
He has always been very supportive. 他一直都非常乐于支持别人。 
People around him trust him a lot. 身边的人都很信任他。 
He is known for his kindness. 他以善良而出名 
具体描述 
He often helps others with their work. 他经常在工作上帮助别人。 
He listens patiently when people have problems. 别人遇到问题时，他会耐心倾听。 
He offers help without being asked. 他常常在没人开口前就主动帮忙。 
He believes small actions can make a difference. 他相信小小的行动也能产生影响。 
He never expects anything in return. 他从不期待回报 
描述感受 
I truly admire his attitude. 我真的很佩服他的态度。 
He inspires me to be more helpful. 他激励我成为更乐于助人的人。 
Being around him makes me feel positive. 和他在一起让我感觉很积极。 
I feel grateful to know someone like him. 认识这样的人让我心怀感激。 
He sets a good example for others. 他为他人树立了很好的榜样。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Someone who often helps others and really impresses me is a close friend of mine named Daniel. I’ve known 
him for several years, and during this time, I’ve seen how naturally helpful he is in daily life. 
Daniel helps others on a regular basis, especially people around him. Whether it’s classmates struggling with 
assignments or friends dealing with personal problems, he’s always willing to step in. He listens patiently, gives 
practical advice, and sometimes even sacrifices his own time to support others. What stands out is that he 
never waits to be asked. He notices when someone needs help and offers it immediately.  
 
 

=== PAGE 47 ===
 
 
47 
 
 
He does this simply because he believes helping others is the right thing to do, not because he wants 
recognition. 
I genuinely admire him for this. Being around someone like Daniel reminds me that kindness doesn’t have to 
be dramatic—it can be quiet and consistent. His behavior has influenced me to pay more attention to people 
around me and to offer help whenever I can. Knowing him makes me feel more positive about human nature, 
and I’m grateful to have such a friend in my life. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Should children help their parents with household chores? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“责任感”“技能培养”“家庭合作”解释为什么应该参与。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, children should help their parents with household chores. Doing small tasks teaches responsibility and 
independence. Children learn that family life needs cooperation. 
Chores also help children develop basic skills, like cleaning and organizing. These skills are useful in daily life. 
Parents should give age-appropriate tasks and guidance. Helping at home should not feel like punishment. 
So, household chores help children grow into responsible and helpful adults. 
 
Question 2: What kind of help do people need when looking for a new job? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从信息、技能和心理支持三个角度展开，解释不同类型的帮助为何重要。 
Sample Answer: 
When looking for a new job, people need different kinds of help. First, they need information about job 
openings and company needs. Clear guidance helps them choose suitable jobs. 
Second, skills support is important, such as writing a resume or preparing for interviews. Many people also 
need training to improve abilities. 
Emotional support matters too, because job searching can be stressful. So, practical advice and encouragement 
are both important. 
 
Question 3: Who should people ask for help, colleagues or family members? 
解题思路：对比 + 情境类问题。重点解释“看问题类型”。 
Sample Answer: 
It depends on the situation. For work-related problems, colleagues are more helpful because they understand 
the job and tasks. 
For personal or emotional problems, family members are better. They know the person well and offer 
emotional support. 
So, people should choose who to ask based on the problem they face.

Event【事】 
给别人建议 
Describe a time when you gave advice to others 
You should say:  
When it was 
To whom you gave the advice 
What the advice was 
And explain why you gave the advice 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是”事件类+人际关系类”话题，要求你描述一次你给别人建议的经历。必须说明：什么时候发生、你给谁建
议、建议内容是什么、以及你为什么要给这个建议。整体以过去时为主，最后可以用现在时总结意义或感受。重点
不是“建议是否专业”，而是动机和影响。 
思路方面 
建议的对象可以是：朋友、同学、家人。内容可以是：学习方法、考试选择、时间管理、情绪调整。关键在于说清
楚：对方当时遇到的困难、你是如何思考并给出建议的、你为什么觉得有必要开口。 
结构方面 
第一段：交代时间和对象，说明当时的背景； 
第二段：具体说明你给了什么建议，以及是如何说的； 
第三段：解释你为什么给这个建议，并总结你的感受或收获。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It happened last year during exam season. 事情发生在去年的考试季。 
I gave advice to my close friend. 我给了我的好朋友建议。 
She was feeling stressed about her studies. 她当时对学习感到压力很大。 
We often share our problems with each other. 我们经常互相分享问题。 
I noticed she was not in a good mood. 我注意到她情绪不太好。 
具体描述 
I suggested she make a simple study plan. 我建议她制定一个简单的学习计划。 
I told her to focus on one task at a time. 我告诉她一次只专注一件事。 
I encouraged her to take short breaks. 我鼓励她适当休息。 
The advice was practical and easy to follow. 这个建议很实用，也容易执行。 
I shared my own experience with her. 我和她分享了自己的经历。 
描述感受 
I wanted to help her feel calmer. 我想帮助她放松下来。 
I felt responsible as her friend. 作为朋友我感到有责任。 
She thanked me for my advice. 她感谢了我的建议。 
I felt glad that I could support her. 我很高兴能支持她。 
This experience made our friendship stronger. 这次经历让我们的友谊更牢固。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A time when I gave advice to others was last year during the final exam period. I gave the advice to my close 
friend, who was feeling very stressed about her studies. She had many exams in a short time and didn’t know 
how to manage her schedule well. 
When she talked to me, I could tell she was tired and worried. I suggested that she make a simple study plan 
instead of trying to do everything at once.  
 
 

=== PAGE 49 ===
 
 
49 
 
 
I told her to focus on one subject each day and set small goals, such as finishing a few pages or doing several 
practice questions. I also encouraged her to take short breaks, because resting could help her stay focused. To 
make my advice clearer, I shared my own experience and explained how this method helped me feel calmer 
during exams. 
I gave her this advice because I really wanted to help her. As her friend, I felt responsible to support her when 
she was under pressure. After following my suggestions for a few days, she told me she felt less stressed and 
more confident. That made me feel very happy and relieved. This experience showed me that even simple 
advice can make a difference, and it also made our friendship stronger. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Should people prepare before giving advice? 
解题思路：观点 + 原因类问题。可以从“责任感”和“建议的影响”入手，解释为什么给建议前需要思考背
景、情况和后果。重点不是“要不要给建议”，而是“准备是否重要”。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think people should prepare before giving advice. Advice can influence others’ decisions, so it should be 
careful and responsible. If people speak without understanding the situation, the advice may be wrong or even 
harmful. 
Preparing helps people think about the other person’s feelings and needs. It also allows them to give more 
practical and useful suggestions. Sometimes listening first is also part of preparation. 
So, preparing before giving advice shows respect and helps others make better choices. 
 
Question 2: Is it good to ask advice from strangers online? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“便利性”和“风险”两个方向展开，说明为什么有些人会向陌生人求助，同
时解释为什么需要保持谨慎。 
Sample Answer: 
Asking advice from strangers online can be helpful, but it also has risks. On the positive side, strangers may give 
different ideas and experiences, especially when friends or family are not available. Some people feel more 
comfortable sharing problems with strangers because there is less pressure. 
However, not all advice online is reliable. Strangers may not understand the full situation, and some 
information can be wrong or unsafe. People also need to protect their privacy. 
So, online advice can be useful, but people should think carefully before trusting it. 
 
Question 3: What are the personalities of people whose job is to give advice to others? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从“倾听能力”“耐心”“责任感”几个角度展开，解释为什么这些性格特征对
“给建议”这一职业很重要。 
Sample Answer: 
People whose job is to give advice usually have calm and patient personalities. They need to listen carefully 
before speaking, so being a good listener is very important. 
They are often understanding and kind, because people come to them with problems or worries. Responsibility 
also matters, since advice can influence others’ decisions. 
So, advisers are usually patient, thoughtful, and careful, which helps them support others in a helpful way. 
 
Question 4: What are the problems if you ask too many people for advice? 
解题思路：原因与影响类问题。可以从“信息冲突”“决策困难”“失去自信”三个角度解释为什么向太多人求
建议反而会带来问题。 
Sample Answer: 
Asking too many people for advice can cause problems. Different people often give different opinions, which 
can make someone feel confused. Instead of helping, too much advice may delay decisions. 
It can also reduce confidence. When people depend too much on others’ ideas, they may stop trusting their 
own judgment. In some cases, people may feel stressed because they want to please everyone. 
So, advice is useful, but asking too many people can lead to confusion and hesitation.

50 
 
 
微笑的场合 
Describe an occasion when many people were smiling 
You should say: 
When it happened  
Who you were with  
What happened  
And explain why most people were smiling 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“经历事件类 + 情绪氛围类”话题，要求你描述一次很多人都在微笑的场合。题目需要你说明：事情发生
在什么时候、你和谁在一起、发生了什么事，以及为什么大多数人都在微笑。整体叙述以过去时为主，最后总结感
受时可以用现在时。重点在于现场氛围和情绪原因。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择毕业典礼、婚礼、生日派对、节日庆祝活动等。思路上可以先说清这个场合的背景和时间；然后重点
可以放在当天发生了什么，以及你观察到大家的表情和反应；最后可以说一说为什么这个场合会让这么多人自然地
露出笑容。 
结构方面 
第一段：交代事情发生的时间、地点，以及你和谁在一起； 
第二段：描述当天具体发生了什么，以及现场情况； 
第三段：解释为什么大多数人都在微笑，并总结你的感受 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It happened during my graduation ceremony. 这发生在我的毕业典礼上。 
The event took place last summer. 这次活动发生在去年夏天。 
I was there with my classmates and teachers. 我和同学、老师一起在那里。 
It was a very important day for us. 那对我们来说是很重要的一天。 
Many people gathered in one place. 很多人聚集在一起。 
具体描述 
People were taking photos and chatting happily. 人们在拍照、开心地聊天。 
The atmosphere was warm and relaxed. 现场气氛温暖而轻松。 
Everyone was dressed nicely. 每个人都穿得很得体。 
We shared memories and talked about the future. 我们一起回忆过去、聊未来。 
Applause and laughter could be heard everywhere. 到处都能听到掌声和笑声。 
描述感受 
Most people were smiling from the heart. 大多数人是发自内心地微笑。 
I felt proud and emotional at the same time. 我既自豪又感动。 
The smiles made the moment unforgettable. 微笑让这一刻难以忘怀。 
It was a moment full of happiness and hope. 那是充满幸福和希望的时刻。 
Even now, I still remember that scene clearly. 直到现在我仍清楚记得那个画面。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
An occasion when I saw many people smiling was during my high school graduation ceremony. It happened last 
summer, and I was there with my classmates, teachers, and family members. It was an important day for all of 
us, because it marked the end of our school life and the beginning of a new stage. 
On that day, everyone gathered in the school hall early in the morning. People were dressed neatly and taking 
photos with friends and teachers. During the ceremony, the head teacher gave a speech, and many students 
received their certificates on the stage.  
 
 

=== PAGE 51 ===
 
 
51 
 
 
I could see smiles on their faces when they walked back to their seats. After the formal part, we talked, hugged 
each other, and shared memories from the past three years. Laughter and applause filled the room, and the 
atmosphere felt warm and relaxed. 
Most people were smiling because we all felt proud of what we had achieved. We had worked hard for years, 
and this day was a reward for our efforts. At the same time, we were excited about the future and new 
opportunities ahead. I felt happy and a little emotional when I saw so many smiling faces around me. Even 
now, when I think about that day, those smiles still stay clearly in my mind. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Do you think people who like to smile are more friendly? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以说明“微笑传递信号”，但也指出“并非绝对”。 
Sample Answer: 
People who like to smile are often seen as more friendly. Smiling makes others feel comfortable and welcome. 
It shows openness and positive feelings. 
However, smiling does not always mean someone is truly friendly. Some people smile out of politeness. Others 
may be quiet but kind. 
So, smiling helps create a friendly image, but true friendliness also depends on actions and behavior. 
 
Question 2: Why do most people smile in photographs? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“习惯”“积极形象”“情绪表达”解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Most people smile in photographs because smiling looks friendly and positive. A smile makes the picture more 
pleasant and shows happiness. 
People also want to leave good memories, especially in family or travel photos. Smiling is a natural habit when 
a camera appears. 
So, smiling helps people feel confident and creates a warm image in photos. 
 
Question 3: Do women smile more than men? Why? 
解题思路：对比 + 原因类问题。可以从社会角色和表达方式解释差异，同时承认个体差异。 
Sample Answer: 
Women are often seen smiling more than men. One reason is that women are encouraged to show emotions 
and be friendly in social situations. Smiling helps communication. 
Men may feel social pressure to appear serious or calm. However, this does not mean men are less friendly. 
Personality matters more than gender. 
So, women may smile more in general, but it depends on the individual. 
 
Question 4: Do people smile more when they are younger or older? 
解题思路：对比 + 观点类问题。可以先给出倾向，再解释原因，同时承认个体差异。 
Sample Answer: 
I think younger people usually smile more. Children have fewer worries and enjoy simple happiness. They laugh 
easily when playing or talking with friends. 
Older people have more responsibilities and stress, so they may smile less. However, some older people smile 
more because they feel calm and satisfied with life. 
So, age matters, but personality also plays an important role. 
 
 

=== PAGE 52 ===

禁用手机的场合 
Describe an occasion when you were not allowed to use your mobile phone 
You should say: 
When it was 
Where it was 
Why you were not allowed to use your mobile phone 
And how you felt about it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“经历事件 + 规则限制类”话题，要求你描述一次你被禁止使用手机的经历。需要说明：事情发生在什么
时候、在哪里、为什么不被允许使用手机，以及你当时的感受。整体以过去时叙述经历，最后可以用现在时总结看
法或反思。重点在于场景、原因和情绪变化。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择考试、课堂、重要会议或某次活动。思路上可以先说清事情发生的时间和地点；接着可以重点说当时
为什么不允许使用手机，是出于规则、公平或专注的考虑；最后可以说一说你当下的不适应，以及后来是否理解这
个规定。 
结构方面 
第一段：交代时间、地点，以及当时的背景； 
第二段：说明为什么不能用手机，以及具体情况； 
第三段：描述你的感受，并总结这次经历带来的想法。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It happened during an important exam. 这件事发生在一次重要考试中。 
I was still in high school at that time. 那时我还在上高中。 
The place was very quiet and serious. 那个地方非常安静严肃。 
Everyone had to follow the same rule. 每个人都必须遵守同样的规则。 
The rule was clearly explained before it started. 规则在开始前就讲清楚了。 
具体描述 
We were asked to turn off our phones. 我们被要求关掉手机。 
All phones had to be left outside the room. 所有手机都要放在教室外。 
Using a phone could lead to serious punishment. 使用手机会有严重后果。 
The rule was made to ensure fairness. 这个规定是为了保证公平。 
I had to rely only on myself. 我只能完全靠自己。 
描述感受 
I felt uncomfortable at first. 一开始我感到不太适应。 
I was a bit nervous without my phone. 没有手机我有点紧张。 
Later, I understood the reason behind it. 后来我理解了背后的原因。 
It helped me focus better. 它反而让我更专注。 
Now I think it was a meaningful experience. 现在我觉得那是一次有意义的经历。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
An occasion when I was not allowed to use my mobile phone was during an important final exam in high 
school. It happened about two years ago in the school examination hall. The environment was very quiet and 
serious, and all students had to follow strict rules. 
Before the exam started, the teacher clearly explained that no one was allowed to use a mobile phone. We 
were asked to turn off our phones and leave them outside the room. If anyone was caught using a phone, the 
exam would be canceled. The reason for this rule was to make sure the exam was fair for everyone. At that 
time, I felt a little uncomfortable because I was used to keeping my phone with me, even if I didn’t use it. 

=== PAGE 53 ===
 
 
53 
 
 
At first, I felt nervous without my phone nearby. It made me realize how much I depended on it in daily life. 
However, as the exam went on, I started to feel more focused. Without my phone, there were no distractions 
at all. I had no choice but to concentrate on the questions and rely on my own knowledge. After the exam, I 
actually felt proud of myself. Looking back now, I think this experience was meaningful. It taught me that 
sometimes being away from my phone can help me stay calm, focused, and more confident in my own abilities. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: How do young and old people use mobile phones differently? 
解题思路：对比类问题。与前面“apps”类似，但可更强调“功能使用差异”。 
Sample Answer: 
Young people use mobile phones for many things, like chatting, watching videos, and playing games. Phones 
are part of their daily life. 
Older people mainly use phones for calls, messages, and payments. They prefer simple functions and clear 
screens. 
So, the difference is in purpose and frequency of use. 
 
Question 2: What positive and negative impact do mobile phones have on friendship? 
解题思路：评估类问题。需要同时解释促进与破坏友谊的原因。 
Sample Answer: 
Mobile phones help friendships by making communication easy. Friends can message or call anytime, even 
when far away. 
However, phones can also harm friendships. People may spend too much time online and ignore friends 
around them. Misunderstandings can happen through messages. 
So, phones strengthen friendships when used well, but too much use can damage real connections. 
 
Question 3: Is it a waste of time to take pictures with mobile phones? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以采取“适度不浪费，过度才浪费”的中立立场。 
Sample Answer: 
I don’t think taking pictures with mobile phones is a waste of time. Photos help people record memories and 
special moments. 
However, if people spend too much time taking pictures instead of enjoying the moment, it can be a problem. 
Balance is important. 
So, taking photos is meaningful when done in moderation. 
 
Question 4: Do you think it is necessary to have laws on the use of mobile phones? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从安全、隐私和公共秩序解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, laws on mobile phone use are necessary. Using phones while driving or walking can be dangerous and 
cause accidents. 
Laws also protect privacy, such as stopping people from taking photos without permission. Clear rules help 
create a safer society. 
So, mobile phone laws guide people to use technology responsibly.

为家人骄傲 
Describe a time when you felt proud of a family member 
You should say: 
When it happened 
Who the person is  
What the person did 
And explain why you felt proud of him or her 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“事件经历类 + 情感类”话题，要求你描述一次你为某位家庭成员感到骄傲的经历。需要说明：事情发生
在什么时候、这个人是谁、他或她做了什么、以及你为什么感到骄傲。整体以过去时叙述经历，结尾可以用现在时
总结感受或意义。重点在于具体行为 + 情感原因。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择父母、兄弟姐妹或祖辈。思路上可以先说清事情发生的时间和背景；然后可以重点说这位家人做了哪
件事，比如坚持、帮助他人、克服困难；最后可以说一说这件事为什么触动你，让你感到骄傲。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍时间和人物，交代基本背景； 
第二段：描述这位家人具体做了什么； 
第三段：解释你为什么感到骄傲，并总结感受 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It happened about two years ago. 这件事发生在大约两年前。 
The person is my mother. 这个人是我的妈妈。 
We were at home at that time. 那时我们在家里。 
It was a difficult period for our family. 那是一段对我们家庭来说很困难的时期。 
I still remember it very clearly. 我现在仍然记得很清楚 
具体描述 
She worked very hard every day. 她每天都非常努力地工作。 
She took care of the family and her job at the same time. 她同时照顾家庭和工作。 
She never complained about the pressure. 她从不抱怨压力。 
She stayed calm and positive. 她一直保持冷静和积极。 
She solved the problem step by step. 她一步一步解决了问题。 
描述感受 
I felt proud of her strength. 我为她的坚强感到骄傲。 
She set a good example for me. 她为我树立了好榜样。 
It made me respect her even more. 这让我更加尊敬她。 
I learned a lot from her attitude. 我从她的态度中学到了很多。 
This memory still gives me confidence. 这个回忆至今仍给我信心。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A time when I felt proud of a family member was about two years ago, during a difficult period for my family. 
The person I felt proud of was my mother. At that time, our family was facing some challenges, and everyone 
felt a lot of pressure. 
During that period, my mother showed great strength and responsibility. She worked very hard every day and 
tried her best to take care of both her job and our family. Even when she was tired, she never complained. 
Instead, she stayed calm and positive, and she always encouraged us not to give up. I remember that she would 
make plans, solve problems step by step, and support everyone emotionally. Her attitude helped our family 
stay together and get through that hard time. 
 
 

=== PAGE 55 ===
 
 
55 
 
 
I felt proud of her because she didn’t run away from difficulties. She faced them directly and handled 
everything with patience and courage. Seeing her effort and calm behavior made me realize what it means to 
be responsible and strong. She set a great example for me, and I learned a lot from her way of dealing with 
stress. Even now, when I face problems in my own life, I often think of her and feel more confident. That is why 
this moment made me truly proud of my mother. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: When would parents feel proud of their children? 
解题思路：原因类问题。重点不是“成绩唯一”，而是多维度解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Parents feel proud when children try their best. Good grades can make parents happy, but effort and 
improvement matter more. 
Parents also feel proud when children are kind, responsible, and respectful. Helping others and behaving well 
show good character. 
So, parents are proud not only of success, but also of attitude and values. 
 
Question 2: Should parents reward children? Why and how? 
解题思路：观点 + 方法类问题。需要解释“为什么奖励”，以及“如何合理奖励”。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, parents should reward children in a proper way. Rewards encourage good behavior and effort. 
Rewards do not need to be expensive. Praise, time together, or small gifts are enough. Parents should focus on 
effort, not only results. 
So, rewards help children feel valued when used wisely. 
 
Question 3: Is it good to reward children too often? Why? 
解题思路：评估类问题。需要说明过度奖励的风险，同时给出合理建议。 
Sample Answer: 
Rewarding children can be helpful, but doing it too often is not good. If children expect rewards all the time, 
they may lose inner motivation. 
They might only do things for gifts, not for responsibility or interest. Rewards should focus on effort, not every 
small action. 
So, rewards are useful when used wisely and in moderation. 
 
Question 4: On what occasions would adults be proud of themselves? 
解题思路：原因与情境类问题。可以从“完成目标”“承担责任”“克服困难”三个角度展开，解释成年人在什
么情况下会产生自我认可，而不仅仅是外在成就。 
Sample Answer: 
Adults often feel proud of themselves when they reach important goals. This can include doing well at work, 
finishing a difficult task, or improving a skill after long effort. 
They may also feel proud when they take responsibility for their family, such as caring for children or 
supporting parents. Overcoming problems, like stress or failure, also brings pride. 
In addition, helping others or making good decisions can give adults a strong sense of achievement. So, pride 
often comes from effort, responsibility, and personal growth.
