自行车or 摩托车or 汽车旅行 
Describe a bicycle or motorcycle or car trip you would like to go  
You should say:  
Who you would like to go with 
Where you would like to go  
When you would like to go 
And explain why you would like to go by bicycle or motorcycle or car 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“事件类 + 交通方式类”话题，要求你描述一次你想进行的骑行或自驾旅行。需要说明：你想和谁一起
去、想去哪里、什么时候去，以及为什么选择这种交通方式。整体以将来时为主，也可以穿插少量现在时表达个人
偏好。重点在于出行方式与旅行体验之间的关系。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择自行车、摩托车或汽车中的一种。思路上可以先说清你想和谁一起去旅行；然后可以说一说目的地和
时间安排；接着重点可以放在为什么选择这种交通方式，比如自由、舒适或沿途风景；最后可以补充这种方式能带
来的感受。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍你想进行的旅行，以及同行的人； 
第二段：说明目的地和时间，并描述行程设想； 
第三段：解释为什么选择这种交通方式，并总结你的期待和感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
I would like to go on a short car trip. 我想进行一次短途自驾游。 
I plan to travel with my close friend. 我打算和一位好朋友一起去。 
It is something I have thought about for a while. 这是我考虑了一段时间的旅行。 
The trip would not be too long. 这次行程不会太长。 
It is more about the experience than the destination. 这次旅行更注重体验而不是目的地。 
具体描述 
I would like to go to a nearby coastal city. 我想去一个附近的海滨城市。 
We would like to go during a public holiday. 我们想在假期去。 
Driving allows us to stop whenever we want. 开车可以让我们随时停车。 
We can enjoy the scenery along the way. 我们可以欣赏沿途风景。 
The journey itself would be relaxing. 旅程本身就会很放松。 
描述感受 
I enjoy the sense of freedom when driving. 我很享受开车带来的自由感。 
It helps me slow down and relax. 它能让我慢下来、放松心情。 
I feel more connected to the places I pass. 我会更有参与感。 
It would be a comfortable and flexible trip. 这会是一趟舒适又灵活的旅行。 
That is why I prefer going by car. 这就是我选择自驾的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A trip I would really like to go on is a short car trip with one of my close friends. We have known each other for 
many years, and we both enjoy traveling in a relaxed way. Instead of joining a tour group, we prefer to plan 
things by ourselves and enjoy the journey step by step. 
I would like to go to a nearby coastal city, which is not too far from where I live. The best time for this trip 
would be during a public holiday or a long weekend, when we are not busy with work or study. We would drive 
along the coast, stop at small towns, and maybe spend some time by the sea. The plan is not very strict, and 
we would decide what to do depending on our mood and the weather. 
 

=== PAGE 57 ===
 
 
57 
 
 
I would like to go by car because it gives me a strong sense of freedom. Driving allows us to stop whenever we 
want, take photos, or simply rest for a while. We can enjoy the scenery along the way instead of rushing to the 
destination. A car trip also feels more comfortable, especially when carrying luggage or buying local food. For 
me, the journey itself is an important part of the travel experience. That is why I would really like to take this 
trip by car and enjoy every moment of it. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Which form of vehicle is more popular in your country, bikes, cars or motorcycles? 
解题思路：比较与说明类问题。可以先给出总体判断，再分别解释不同交通工具受欢迎或不受欢迎的原因，比
如生活节奏、城市结构、收入水平和使用场景，从而说明“主流选择”是如何形成的。 
Sample Answer: 
In my country, cars are the most popular form of vehicle. Many families choose cars because they are 
comfortable and convenient, especially for long trips or traveling with family members. Cars also protect 
people from bad weather, which is important in daily life. 
Bikes are still common in cities for short distances. They are cheap, healthy, and good for the environment, but 
they are not suitable for long travel. Motorcycles are less popular, as they are seen as less safe. 
So overall, cars are the main choice, while bikes and motorcycles are used in specific situations. 
 
Question 2: Do you think air pollution comes mostly from mobile vehicles? 
解题思路：观点 + 原因类问题。可以先给出自己的总体看法，再从“车辆确实是重要来源”与“并非唯一来
源”两个方面展开，重点解释不同污染来源在现实生活中的作用，从而体现观点的平衡性。 
Sample Answer: 
I think mobile vehicles are an important source of air pollution, but they are not the only one. Cars, buses, and 
trucks produce exhaust gas, especially in big cities with heavy traffic. This makes the air dirty and unhealthy. 
However, factories and power plants also cause serious pollution. Burning coal and other fuels releases a large 
amount of smoke and harmful gases. Construction work can also add dust to the air. 
So, while vehicles play a big role in air pollution, the problem comes from many sources, not just traffic. 
 
Question 3: Do you think people need to change the way of transportation drastically to protect the 
environment? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以先给出总体态度，再解释“是否需要彻底改变”，重点放在“逐步改变更现实”。
说明为什么交通方式与环境有关，同时解释人们在生活便利和环保之间需要平衡。 
Sample Answer: 
I think people need to change the way of transportation, but not in a very drastic way. Transportation is a major 
cause of pollution, so change is necessary. Using public transport, bicycles, or electric vehicles can reduce 
harmful gas and protect the environment. 
However, a sudden and complete change is not realistic for everyone. Some people rely on cars for work or 
family needs. It takes time to build better public transport and new habits. 
So, gradual changes with support from the government and society are more practical and effective for 
protecting the environment. 
 
Question 4: How are the transportation systems in urban areas and rural areas different? 
解题思路：对比类问题。可以从“交通种类”“便利程度”“基础设施”进行对比，并解释这些差异与人口密度
和经济发展有关。 
Sample Answer: 
Transportation systems in urban and rural areas are quite different. In cities, people have many choices, such as 
buses, subways, taxis, and shared bikes. Transport is frequent and convenient because many people need it 
every day. 
In rural areas, transportation is more limited. Public transport is less common, and people often rely on private 
cars or motorcycles. Roads may be fewer and travel time is longer. 
So, cities offer more developed transport systems, while rural areas depend more on personal vehicles due to 
lower population and demand. 
 
 

=== PAGE 58 ===
 
 
58 
 
 
 
发挥想象力 
Describe a time you needed to use your imagination 
You should say: 
When it was 
Why you needed to use imagination 
How difficult or easy it was 
And explain how you felt about it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“事件经历类 + 思维能力类”题目，要求你描述一次你必须动用想象力的经历。题目中的关键词是 use 
your imagination，并不一定指艺术创作，也可以是解决问题、完成任务或应对突发情况。回答时需要交代时间、原
因、难度以及你的情绪体验。整体时态以过去时为主。 
思路方面 
你可以选择学习、工作或日常生活中的场景，比如写故事、做演示、设计活动、临时编一个解释或解决方案等。重
点在于说明“为什么常规方法不够用，必须靠想象力”，以及你在过程中是否感到吃力或反而很投入。情绪部分可
以从紧张、压力过大，转向成就感或轻松感。 
结构方面 
第一段交代事情发生的时间和背景，引出需要用想象力的情境。 
第二段重点描述你具体是如何运用想象力的，以及这个过程是否困难。 
第三段总结你的感受和这次经历对你的启发 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It happened during my university years. 这件事发生在我大学期间。 
I was under a tight deadline. 当时我时间非常紧。 
The task required creative thinking. 这个任务需要创造性思维。 
I didn’t have enough information at first. 起初我掌握的信息并不充分。 
It was part of a group assignment. 这是一次小组作业的一部分。 
具体描述 
I had to come up with ideas quickly. 我必须迅速想出点子。 
I imagined different situations and outcomes. 我设想了不同的情境和结果。 
There was no fixed answer. 这件事并没有标准答案。 
I tried several ideas before choosing one. 我尝试了好几种想法才做决定。 
It was more challenging than I expected. 这比我预想的要更有挑战。 
描述感受 
At first, I felt a bit stressed. 一开始我有点紧张。 
Gradually, I started to enjoy the process. 慢慢地，我开始享受这个过程。 
It gave me a strong sense of achievement. 它给了我很强的成就感。 
I felt proud of myself afterward. 事后我对自己感到很自豪。 
That experience boosted my confidence. 那次经历增强了我的自信心。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Back in my university days, there was a time when I really needed to use my imagination for a group 
presentation. We were asked to design a short scenario to explain an abstract concept, but there were no 
examples or clear guidelines given. 
Because of the limited instructions, I had to imagine a real-life situation that everyone could understand. I 
thought about daily experiences, possible characters, and how the story could naturally connect to the topic. 
At the beginning, it felt quite difficult, since I wasn’t used to creative tasks like this.  
 

=== PAGE 59 ===
 
 
59 
 
 
However, after brainstorming for a while, ideas started to come more easily. I tried several different versions 
before settling on the final one. 
Although the process was challenging, I gradually found it enjoyable. Creating something from scratch made 
me feel more involved in the task. When our presentation was well received by the class, I felt a strong sense of 
satisfaction. That experience showed me that imagination isn’t just for artists-it’s also useful in problem-solving 
and communication. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Do you think adults can have lots of imagination? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以反驳“想象力只属于孩子”，并解释经验如何转化为创造力。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think adults can have lots of imagination. Although children imagine freely, adults use experience to 
create new ideas. Imagination does not disappear with age. 
Adults show imagination in work, art, and problem solving. They imagine better ways to do things and create 
useful solutions. 
However, stress and routine may reduce imagination. When adults relax and try new things, their imagination 
becomes active again. 
So, adults can be imaginative, especially when they keep curiosity and openness. 
 
Question 2: Do you think imagination is essential for scientists? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以先给出肯定态度，再解释想象力如何帮助科学家提出问题和解决问题。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think imagination is essential for scientists. Imagination helps scientists think beyond what they already 
know. It allows them to ask new questions and imagine possible results. 
When scientists face problems, imagination helps them find creative solutions. It is also useful when they 
design experiments or explain ideas. 
Of course, imagination must work with facts and testing. But without imagination, scientific progress would be 
very slow. 
So, imagination is an important part of scientific work. 
 
Question 3: What kinds of jobs need imagination? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从创意、解决问题和设计类职业展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Many jobs need imagination. Artists, designers, and writers use imagination to create new ideas. 
Imagination is also important for scientists and engineers when solving problems or designing products. 
Teachers need imagination to make lessons interesting. 
So, imagination is useful not only in art, but also in many practical jobs. 
 
Question 4: What subjects are helpful for children’s imagination? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从艺术类与综合能力类学科展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Subjects like art and music are very helpful for children’s imagination. Drawing, painting, and music allow 
children to express ideas freely. 
Literature and storytelling also help imagination. Reading stories encourages children to imagine different 
worlds and characters. Even science can help imagination by asking questions and solving problems. 
So, creative and thinking-based subjects are important for developing imagination. 
 
 

=== PAGE 60 ===
 
 
60 
 
 
鼓励别人做不愿做的事 
Describe a time when you encouraged someone to do something that he or she didn’t want to do 
You should say: 
Who he or she is 
What you encouraged him or her to do 
How he or she reacted 
And explain why you encouraged him or her to do it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“事件经历 + 人际互动”题目，重点在于你主动影响他人行为的经历。题干中的关键词是 encouraged 
someone 和 didn’t want to do，说明对方一开始是抗拒的，而你起到了推动作用。回答时需要交代人物关系、你鼓
励的具体事情、对方的反应，以及你这样做的原因。整体时态以过去时为主。 
思路方面 
可以选择一个真实、生活化的场景，比如鼓励朋友参加比赛、尝试公开表达、换一种学习方式或面对一个挑战。重
点不在“你有多厉害”，而在于你为什么觉得这件事对对方有好处，以及你是如何一步步说服或支持对方的。对方
的反应可以从犹豫、抗拒到慢慢接受，体现过程变化。 
结构方面 
第一段介绍这个人是谁，以及当时的背景情况。 
第二段描述你具体鼓励他或她做什么，以及对方最初和之后的反应。 
第三段解释你鼓励的原因，并补充你对这次经历的感受或反思。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
He is a close friend of mine. 他是我的一位好朋友。 
This happened during our university years. 这件事发生在大学期间。 
He was facing a difficult choice at the time. 当时他正面临一个艰难的选择。 
He lacked confidence in himself. 他对自己缺乏信心。 
I knew him very well. 我对他非常了解。 
具体描述 
I encouraged him to step out of his comfort zone. 我鼓励他走出舒适区。 
He was reluctant at first. 一开始他是抗拒的。 
I explained the benefits patiently. 我耐心地向他解释好处。 
Gradually, his attitude started to change. 慢慢地，他的态度开始改变。 
In the end, he agreed to give it a try. 最后他同意尝试一下。 
描述感受 
I felt relieved when he accepted my advice. 当他接受我的建议时，我感到很欣慰。 
It made me realize the importance of support. 这让我意识到支持他人的重要性。 
I was proud of him for trying. 我为他愿意尝试而感到骄傲。 
The experience strengthened our friendship. 这次经历加深了我们的友谊。 
I felt it was the right thing to do. 我觉得自己这样做是对的。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Back in university, there was a time when I encouraged a close friend of mine to take part in a public speaking 
competition. He had strong ideas but hated speaking in front of people, so he immediately rejected the idea 
when I first mentioned it. 
At that time, I encouraged him to step out of his comfort zone because I believed this experience could help 
him build confidence. He was clearly reluctant at first and kept saying he wasn’t good enough. Instead of 
pushing him too hard, I explained the benefits patiently and told him that trying was more important than 
winning. Gradually, his attitude started to change, and he agreed to give it a try. 
 

=== PAGE 61 ===
 
 
61 
 
 
 
Although he was very nervous on the day of the competition, he managed to finish his speech. Watching him 
stand on stage made me feel proud. I encouraged him because I knew avoiding challenges would only limit 
him. In the end, the experience helped him grow, and it also strengthened our friendship. Looking back, I truly 
believe encouraging him was the right decision. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: How can leaders encourage their employees? 
解题思路：解决方式类问题。可以从“沟通”“认可”“支持发展”三个方面解释具体做法。 
Sample Answer: 
Leaders can encourage employees by showing respect and support. Simple praise for good work helps 
employees feel valued and confident. 
Clear communication is also important. When employees understand goals, they work better. Leaders should 
listen to ideas and concerns. 
Offering learning chances and fair rewards motivates people to improve. A positive work environment builds 
trust and teamwork. 
So, encouragement comes from respect, communication, and opportunities to grow. 
 
Question 2: When should parents encourage their children? 
解题思路：情境与原因类问题。可以从“努力过程”“面对困难”“进步阶段”解释鼓励的合适时机。 
Sample Answer: 
Parents should encourage children when they make effort, not only when they succeed. Encouragement helps 
children feel confident and willing to try again. 
When children face difficulties or feel frustrated, support is especially important. It helps them stay positive 
and learn from mistakes. 
Parents should also encourage children when they show improvement, even small progress. 
So, encouragement should be given during effort, challenges, and growth, not only after success. 
 
Question 3: What kind of encouragement should parents give? 
解题思路：解决方式类问题。可以从“关注努力”“具体鼓励”“情感支持”展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Parents should give encouragement that focuses on effort, not only results. Praising hard work helps children 
stay confident. 
Encouragement should be clear and honest, such as kind words or time spent together. Parents should also 
support children when they fail. 
So, good encouragement builds confidence and motivation, not pressure. 
 
Question 4: Do you think some people are better than others at persuading? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从学习、文化认同和体验感展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think some people are better at persuading than others. Good communicators know how to listen and 
understand others’ feelings. This helps them choose the right words. 
Experience also matters. People who often talk in public or work in teams usually persuade better. Confidence 
and clear thinking are important too. 
So, persuasion is a skill that some people have naturally, but it can also be learned and improved. 
 
 

=== PAGE 62 ===
 
 
62 
 
 
Place【地】 
外国的短期停留 
Describe a foreign country you would like to stay or work for a short period of time 
You should say: 
Which country it is 
Where you got to know this country 
What you will do there 
Why you will stay or work there just for a short period of time 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是“地点类+国家类”话题，要求你描述一个你想短期停留或工作的外国国家。必须说明：是哪个国家、你从哪
里了解到它、你打算在那里做什么、以及为什么只想短期停留。时态以将来时和现在时为主。重点不在长期移民，
而在“短期体验”的合理性。 
思路方面 
可以选择英语国家或生活节奏不同的国家，如新加坡、澳大利亚、日本。内容可包括：短期学习、实习、语言提
升、文化体验。要强调“为什么短期更合适”，例如文化差异、家庭原因、学习目标明确。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍国家，以及你是如何知道这个国家的； 
第二段：说明你计划在那里做什么； 
第三段：解释为什么只选择短期停留，并总结感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The country I would like to stay in is Australia. 我想短期停留的国家是澳大利亚。 
I learned about this country from school and TV programs. 我从学校和电视节目中了解到这个国
家。 
It is famous for its natural environment. 它以自然环境闻名。 
Many people speak English there. 那里很多人说英语。 
It is a popular place for short-term study or work. 它是短期学习或工作的热门国家。 
具体描述 
I would like to work part-time or take a short course. 我想做兼职或上短期课程。 
I want to improve my English skills. 我想提升英语能力。 
I plan to experience local culture and daily life. 我计划体验当地文化和日常生活。 
I would also like to travel to nearby cities. 我也想去附近城市旅行。 
The pace of life there seems relaxed. 那里的生活节奏看起来很放松。 
描述感受 
I think a short stay is more suitable for me. 我觉得短期停留更适合我。 
It would be a good chance to learn and grow. 这是一次学习和成长的好机会。 
I don’t feel ready to live abroad for a long time. 我还没准备好长期在国外生活。 
This experience can broaden my views. 这段经历可以拓宽我的视野。 
I feel excited when I think about this plan. 一想到这个计划我就很兴奋。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A foreign country I would like to stay and work in for a short period of time is Australia. I first learned about this 
country at school and later from TV programs and social media. Many people say Australia has a relaxed 
lifestyle and a beautiful natural environment, which really attracts me. 
 
 

=== PAGE 63 ===
 
 
63 
 
 
If I have the chance, I would like to stay there for a few months. During that time, I hope to take a short English 
course and also find a part-time job, such as working in a café or a small shop. This would allow me to practice 
English in real situations and understand how people work and communicate there. In my free time, I would 
like to travel to nearby cities and enjoy nature, such as beaches and parks. I think this kind of daily experience 
is very different from just being a tourist. 
I only want to stay or work there for a short period of time because I see it as a learning experience rather than 
a long-term plan. I still want to come back to my own country to continue my studies and stay close to my 
family. A short stay feels less stressful and more realistic for me. I believe this experience would help me 
become more confident, improve my English, and broaden my views. That is why Australia is the country I 
would like to stay in for a short time. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Why do people sometimes go to other cities or other countries to travel? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“新体验”“放松”“文化差异”三个角度展开，解释人们为什么选择远行而不
是待在原地。 
Sample Answer: 
People travel to other cities or countries to experience new things. Different places offer new food, culture, and 
ways of life, which makes travel exciting. 
Traveling also helps people relax and forget stress from work or study. Being in a new environment can refresh 
the mind. Some people also travel to learn history or improve language skills. 
So, travel gives people new experiences, relaxation, and a wider view of the world. 
 
 

=== PAGE 64 ===
 
 
64 
 
 
家里放松的地方 
Describe your favorite place in your house where you can relax 
You should say: 
Where it is 
What it is like 
What you enjoy doing there 
And explain why you feel relaxed at this place 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“地点类 + 生活方式类”话题，要求你描述家中一个让你放松的地方。需要说明：它在哪里、是什么样
子、你在那儿做什么，以及为什么在那里会感到放松。整体以现在时为主，必要时可简单提及过去习惯。重点在于
空间细节 + 放松原因。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择卧室的一角、阳台、书房或客厅。思路上可以先说清具体位置；然后可以说一说这个地方的环境特
点，比如光线、安静程度；接着重点可以放在你在那儿做的事情；最后说明这些因素为什么能让你放松。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这个地方在哪里，以及整体感觉； 
第二段：描述它的样子和你常做的事情； 
第三段：解释为什么你在这里会感到放松，并总结感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
My favorite place in my house is my bedroom. 我家里最喜欢的地方是我的卧室。 
It is a small but comfortable space. 它不大，但很舒适。 
It is located at the quiet side of the house. 它在房子比较安静的一侧。 
I spend most of my free time there. 我大部分空闲时间都在那里度过。 
It feels private and peaceful. 那里很私密、很安静。 
具体描述 
The room has soft lighting and light colors. 房间有柔和的灯光和浅色调。 
There is a desk, a bed, and a small bookshelf. 有书桌、床和小书架。 
I like sitting there to read or listen to music. 我喜欢在那里读书或听音乐。 
Sometimes I write down my thoughts. 有时我会写下自己的想法。 
I also enjoy doing nothing and resting my mind. 我也享受什么都不做，让大脑休息。 
描述感受 
I feel calm and relaxed there. 我在那里感到平静和放松。 
It helps me forget the stress from daily life. 它让我忘记日常生活的压力。 
I feel safe and comfortable in this space. 在这个空间里我感到安全、舒适。 
It gives me time to be alone with myself. 它给了我独处的时间。 
That’s why it is my favorite place to relax. 这就是它成为我最放松之地的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
My favorite place in my house where I can relax is my bedroom. It is located on the quiet side of the house, 
away from the living room and the street. Although it is not very big, it feels warm and comfortable, and it is a 
place that truly belongs to me. 
The room is simple and tidy, with light-colored walls and soft lighting. There is a bed near the window, a small 
desk, and a bookshelf with some novels and magazines. I enjoy spending time there after a long day. Most of 
the time, I sit on my bed to read or listen to music. Sometimes I write down my thoughts or plan my schedule 
for the next day. On weekends, I like to stay there quietly and do nothing, just letting my mind rest. 
 
 

=== PAGE 65 ===
 
 
65 
 
 
 
I feel relaxed in this place because it is calm and private. No one disturbs me, and I can decide how to spend my 
time. Being in my bedroom helps me forget the stress from study and daily life. It gives me a sense of comfort 
and safety, and I feel free to be myself there. That is why my bedroom is my favorite place in the house to relax 
and recharge. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Why is it difficult for some people to relax? 
解题思路：原因类问题。重点解释“心理”和“生活节奏”的影响。 
Sample Answer: 
Some people find it hard to relax because they feel stressed about work, study, or money. They may keep 
thinking about problems even when resting. 
Modern life is fast, and people use phones all the time, which makes it harder to calm down. Some also worry 
too much about the future. 
So, stress and busy lifestyles make relaxation difficult. 
 
Question 2: What are the benefits of doing exercise? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可从身体、心理、社交三个层面展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Doing exercise has many benefits. It keeps the body healthy and strong and helps people control weight. 
Exercise also improves sleep and energy levels. 
Mentally, exercise reduces stress and makes people feel happier. It can also be a social activity, like playing 
sports with friends. 
So, exercise benefits both the body and mind and improves overall quality of life. 
 
Question 3: Do people in your country exercise after work? 
解题思路：事实 + 说明类问题。可以说明“部分人会”，并解释影响因素。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, many people exercise after work in my country. Some go jogging, others visit gyms or play sports with 
friends. Exercise helps them relax after a busy day. 
However, not everyone does. Some people feel too tired or have family duties. Time and energy influence this 
choice. 
So, exercise after work is common, but not for everyone. 
 
Question 4: What is the place where people spend most of their time at home? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以结合现代生活方式解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Most people spend the most time in the living room or bedroom. The living room is where families relax, watch 
TV, and talk together. 
The bedroom is also important, as people sleep, rest, and use phones there. After a long day, people want a 
private and comfortable space. 
So, living rooms and bedrooms are the main places people stay at home. 
 
 

=== PAGE 66 ===
 
 
66 
 
 
商场 
Describe a shopping mall 
You should say: 
What its name is 
Where it is 
How often you visit it 
And what you usually buy at the mall 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“地点类 + 日常生活类”话题，要求你描述一个购物中心。需要说明：它的名字、位置、你去的频率，以
及你通常在那里买什么。整体以现在时为主，必要时可简单提及过去的习惯。重点在于具体信息 + 个人使用体验。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择你最常去、最熟悉的商场。思路上可以先说清商场的名字和所在位置；然后可以说一说你多久去一
次；接着重点可以放在你通常在那里购买的东西，以及为什么会选择这个商场。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍商场的名字和位置； 
第二段：说明你去的频率以及商场的整体感觉； 
第三段：描述你通常购买的东西，并解释你喜欢这个商场的原因。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The shopping mall I want to describe is called City Center Mall. 我想描述的购物中心叫城市中心商
场。 
It is located near my home. 它在我家附近。 
It is easy to get there by bus or subway. 坐公交或地铁都很方便。 
It is one of the most popular malls in the area. 它是这一带很受欢迎的商场之一。 
I have been going there for years. 我已经去那里很多年了。 
具体描述 
I usually visit it once or twice a month. 我通常一个月去一到两次。 
The mall is large and well-organized. 商场很大，也很有秩序。 
There are many shops and restaurants. 里面有很多商店和餐厅。 
I often spend a few hours there. 我经常在那里待上几个小时。 
It is a good place to relax and shop. 那是一个既能购物又能放松的地方。 
描述感受 
I usually buy clothes and daily items there. 我通常在那里买衣服和日用品。 
Sometimes I buy books or gifts. 有时我也会买书或礼物。 
I enjoy walking around and looking at new products. 我喜欢逛一逛、看看新产品。 
Shopping there feels convenient and comfortable. 在那里购物很方便也很舒适。 
That is why I often choose this mall. 这就是我经常选择它的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
The shopping mall I would like to describe is called City Center Mall. It is located near my home, only about 
fifteen minutes away by bus. Because of its convenient location, it has become one of the places I visit most 
often in my daily life. 
I usually go to this mall once or twice a month, especially on weekends. The mall is quite large and clean, with 
clear signs that make it easy to find different shops. There are many clothing stores, supermarkets, and 
restaurants inside. Sometimes I go there alone, and sometimes I go with my family or friends. Even when I 
don’t plan to buy much, I still enjoy walking around and spending some relaxed time there. 
When I visit the mall, I usually buy clothes, shoes, or daily items such as snacks and household products. If I 
have a special occasion, I may also look for gifts or books.  
 

=== PAGE 67 ===
 
 
67 
 
 
I like this mall because it has almost everything I need in one place, which saves me time and energy. The 
environment is comfortable, and the service is generally good. For me, it is not only a place to shop, but also a 
place to relax and enjoy my free time. That is why City Center Mall is a shopping mall I often visit and really like. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Why do people buy things they don’t need? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“情绪影响”“广告与促销”“社会比较”三个角度展开，重点解释人们在非理
性状态下做出购买决定的原因，而不是简单归结为浪费。 
Sample Answer: 
People often buy things they don’t need for several reasons. One common reason is emotion. When people 
feel bored, stressed, or unhappy, shopping can make them feel better for a short time. 
Advertising also plays an important role. Discounts, sales, and attractive ads make people believe they need 
something right now. In addition, social media and friends’ influence can create pressure to buy similar 
products. 
Sometimes people buy things just because they look nice or new. So, emotions, marketing, and social influence 
often lead people to buy more than they really need. 
 
Question 2: Do you think it’s a waste of time to go shopping? 
解题思路：观点 + 评估类问题。可以先明确态度，再从“购物目的不同”“情绪与社交价值”两个角度解释为什
么购物不一定是浪费时间，关键在于方式和频率。 
Sample Answer: 
I don’t think going shopping is always a waste of time. When people shop with a clear purpose, such as buying 
daily needs or clothes, it is necessary and useful. Shopping helps people prepare for daily life. 
For some people, shopping is also a way to relax. They enjoy looking around, spending time with friends, and 
taking a break from work or study. However, shopping can become a waste of time if people do it too often 
without real needs. 
So, shopping is not a waste of time by itself. It depends on why and how people shop. 
 
Question 3: Why are some people keen on shopping? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“情绪调节”“社会与习惯影响”“便利与刺激”三个角度展开，重点解释购物
为何能带来短期满足感，以及外部因素如何放大这种行为。 
Sample Answer: 
Some people are keen on shopping for several reasons. One main reason is emotion. Shopping can make 
people feel happy and relaxed, especially when they feel stressed or bored. Buying new things gives a short 
sense of pleasure. 
Another reason is habit and social influence. Sales, discounts, and online ads encourage people to shop more 
often. Seeing friends buy new items can also create a strong desire to follow. 
Shopping is also very convenient today. Online stores are easy to use and available at any time. So, emotion, 
influence, and convenience make shopping attractive to many people. 
 
Question 4: What kind of people like shopping? 
解题思路：说明与原因类问题。可以从“性格特点”“生活方式”“情绪需求”三个角度展开，解释哪些类型的
人更容易喜欢购物，以及购物能满足他们什么需求，而不是简单贴标签。 
英文回答： 
Sample Answer: 
People who like shopping often enjoy new experiences and changes. They are usually curious and interested in 
new products, fashion, or trends. Shopping makes them feel excited and satisfied. 
Some people like shopping because it helps them relax. After work or study, shopping can reduce stress and 
improve mood. Social people also enjoy shopping with friends, as it gives them time to talk and share ideas. 
In addition, people who care about appearance or lifestyle may shop more often. So, personality, emotion, and 
social habits all influence who likes shopping. 
 
 

=== PAGE 68 ===
 
 
68 
 
 
Object【物品】 
想拥有的科技产品 
Describe a piece of technology (not a phone) that you would like to own 
You should say: 
What it is 
How much it costs 
How you knew it 
And explain why you would like to own it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“物品 + 观点类”的题目，要求你描述一件你想拥有的科技产品，而且明确说明不能是手机。题目需要你
覆盖四个要点：这项科技是什么、价格大概多少、你是如何知道它的，以及你为什么想拥有它。整体时态以一般现
在时为主，提到了解过程时可以使用过去时。 
思路方面 
你可以选择一种和学习、生活效率或兴趣相关的科技产品，比如降噪耳机、智能手表、电子阅读器、智能扫地机器
人等。重点不在于技术细节，而在于它如何改善你的生活体验。价格不需要非常精确，大致区间即可。说明你是通
过朋友推荐、广告、视频测评或亲身体验了解到它的。 
结构方面 
第一段介绍这项科技产品是什么，以及你是从哪里知道它的。 
第二段补充价格信息，并简单描述它的主要功能或使用场景。 
第三段重点解释你为什么想拥有它，以及它能给你带来的改变和感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
I first learned about it from an online review. 我最早是通过一篇测评了解到它的。 
It’s a piece of technology designed for daily use. 这是一款为日常生活设计的科技产品。 
A close friend recommended it to me. 是一位好朋友推荐给我的。 
I saw it featured in a technology video. 我在科技类视频中看到过它。 
It has become quite popular in recent years. 近几年它变得相当流行。 
具体描述 
It costs around 2,000 yuan. 它的价格大概在两千元左右。 
The design looks simple but modern. 设计简洁而现代。 
It’s mainly used to reduce background noise. 它主要用于降低环境噪音。 
The battery can last for many hours. 它的续航时间很长。 
It’s suitable for both work and relaxation. 既适合工作，也适合放松。 
描述感受 
I think it would greatly improve my daily efficiency. 我觉得它能大大提升我的日常效率。 
It would help me focus better. 它能帮助我更专注。 
I feel it’s worth the money. 我觉得这个价格是值得的。 
Owning it would make my life more comfortable. 拥有它会让生活更舒适。 
I’ve wanted it for a long time. 我已经想要它很久了 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Something I would really like to own is a pair of high-quality noise-cancelling headphones. I first learned about 
this kind of technology from online reviews and videos shared by tech bloggers, and later a close friend 
recommended a specific model to me. 
 
 

=== PAGE 69 ===
 
 
69 
 
 
The headphones cost around 2,000 yuan, which is not cheap, but still reasonable for what they offer. They are 
designed to block out background noise, making them ideal for studying, working, or traveling. The design 
looks modern and comfortable, and the battery can last for many hours, which is perfect for long days. 
What attracts me most is how much they could improve my focus. I often study or work in places with a lot of 
noise, and I find it hard to concentrate. These headphones would create a quiet space for me and help me stay 
productive. I also think they would be great for relaxing with music after a busy day. 
Overall, owning this piece of technology would make my daily life more efficient and comfortable, which is why 
I really want to have it. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: What are the differences between the technology of the past and that of today? 
解题思路：对比类问题。可以从“速度”“便利性”“功能数量”进行对比，并解释为什么现代科技对生活影响
更大。 
Sample Answer: 
Technology today is very different from the past. In the past, machines were simple and worked slowly. People 
used letters, radios, and basic tools. 
Today, technology is fast and smart. Smartphones, computers, and the internet help people communicate and 
work easily. Many tasks can be done in seconds. 
So, modern technology is more powerful and convenient, and it has changed daily life greatly. 
 
Question 2: What technology do young people like to use? 
解题思路：说明与原因类问题。可以从“日常使用频率”“社交与娱乐需求”“学习与便利性”三个角度展开，
解释为什么这些技术对年轻人有吸引力，而不仅是简单列举设备名称。 
Sample Answer: 
Young people like to use many kinds of technology, especially smartphones and the internet. Smartphones are 
used every day for chatting, watching videos, listening to music, and shopping online. Social media apps are 
very popular because they help young people stay connected with friends and share their lives. 
Young people also enjoy using laptops and tablets for study and entertainment. Online learning platforms, 
games, and short videos are common. Some young people like smart devices, such as wireless earphones and 
smart watches, because they are convenient. 
So, young people prefer technology that is fast, fun, and easy to use in daily life. 
 
Question 3: What are the differences between online and face-to-face communication? 
解题思路：对比类问题。可以从“情感表达”“沟通效率”“误解风险”展开，解释两种交流方式在真实感和便
利性上的差异。 
Sample Answer: 
Online communication is fast and convenient. People can send messages anytime and talk with others far 
away. It saves time and is useful for work and daily contact. 
Face-to-face communication feels more real. People can see facial expressions, body language, and tone of 
voice, which helps avoid misunderstanding. It is also easier to build trust and emotional connection. 
So, online communication is efficient, while face-to-face communication is warmer and clearer in expressing 
feelings. 
 
Question 4: Do you think technology has changed the way people communicate? 
解题思路：观点 + 影响类问题。可以先给出肯定态度，再从“速度与便利性”“沟通方式变化”“潜在问题”三
个方面展开，重点解释科技如何改变人们交流的频率、形式和质量，而不是只说“更方便”。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, I think technology has greatly changed the way people communicate. Today, people can send messages, 
make video calls, and share information instantly through phones and apps. This makes communication faster 
and easier, especially for people who live far away. 
Technology also allows people to stay connected all the time, which helps with work and daily life. However, it 
has some problems. People may rely too much on online messages and spend less time talking face to face. 
This can reduce real emotional connection. 
So, technology improves communication efficiency, but people still need to balance it with real-life interaction. 

=== PAGE 70 ===
 
 
70 
 
 
生活中离不开的东西 
Describe something that you can’t live without (not a computer/phone) 
You should say: 
What it is 
What you do with it 
How it helps you in your life 
And explain why you can’t live without it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是“物品类 + 生活习惯类”话题，要求你描述一件不是电脑或手机、但你生活中离不开的东西。需要说明：它是
什么、你用它做什么、它如何帮助你的生活、以及为什么你觉得没有它不行。时态以现在时为主，介绍开始使用的
背景时可用过去时。重点在于使用场景和个人依赖原因。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择生活中真实而具体的物品，比如水杯、笔记本、背包、手表等。思路上可以先说清这件东西是什么，
以及你平时如何使用；然后可以重点说它在健康、效率或情绪上的帮助；最后说明为什么它已经成为你生活中不可
缺少的一部分。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这件东西是什么，以及你从什么时候开始使用； 
第二段：说明你具体用它做什么，它如何帮助你的日常生活； 
第三段：解释为什么你离不开它，并总结感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The thing I can’t live without is my water bottle. 我离不开的东西是我的水杯。 
I have been using it for several years. 我已经用了它好几年。 
It is something I carry with me every day. 它是我每天随身携带的东西。 
I started using it to stay healthy. 我开始用它是为了保持健康。 
It may look simple, but it is very important to me. 它看起来很简单，但对我很重要。 
具体描述 
I use it to drink water throughout the day. 我整天用它喝水。 
It reminds me to stay hydrated. 它提醒我多喝水。 
I bring it to school and when I go out. 我上学和外出都会带着它。 
It helps me avoid buying bottled drinks. 它让我避免买瓶装饮料。 
It is easy to carry and clean. 它方便携带，也容易清洗。 
描述感受 
It helps me build a healthy habit. 它帮我养成健康习惯。 
I feel uncomfortable when I forget it. 忘带它我会不太舒服。 
It makes my daily life more organized. 它让我的日常生活更有条理。 
I feel more energetic when I drink enough water. 喝够水我会更有精力。 
That’s why I can’t imagine life without it. 这就是我无法想象没有它的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Something that I can’t live without is my water bottle. I have been using it for several years, and I carry it with 
me almost everywhere. It may seem like a very simple object, but it plays an important role in my daily life. 
I use my water bottle to drink water throughout the day, especially when I am studying or going out. It reminds 
me to stay hydrated, because I can easily forget to drink enough water when I am busy. I usually bring it to 
school, the library, or even when I take a walk. Having it with me also helps me avoid buying bottled drinks, 
which is better for both my health and the environment. The bottle is light, easy to carry, and simple to clean, 
so it is very convenient to use. 
 

=== PAGE 71 ===
 
 
71 
 
 
 
I feel that this water bottle helps me build a healthy habit. When I drink enough water, I feel more energetic 
and focused. On days when I forget to bring it, I feel uncomfortable and less active. Over time, it has become 
part of my routine, just like brushing my teeth or eating meals. That is why I think I can’t live without it. It 
supports my health in a small but meaningful way, and it makes my daily life easier and more organized. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Why are children attracted to new things (such as electronics)? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从好奇心、刺激感和新鲜体验来解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Children are attracted to new things because they are curious about the world. New electronics have bright 
colors, sounds, and movement, which catch attention easily. 
They also offer fun and instant feedback, like games or videos. Children enjoy exploring and learning through 
new experiences. 
So, curiosity and excitement make new things very attractive to children. 
 
Question 2: Why do some grown-ups hate to throw out old things (such as clothes)? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“情感价值”“习惯”“浪费心理”展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Some grown-ups hate to throw out old things because of emotional attachment. Old clothes or objects often 
remind them of memories or important times. 
They may also believe that throwing things away is wasteful, especially if the item still works. Habit also plays a 
role, as keeping things feels safe. 
So, feelings, habits, and values make people keep old items. 
 
Question 3: Is the way people buy things affected? How? 
解题思路：影响类问题。可以从科技发展和消费习惯变化解释“怎么买”发生了改变。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, the way people buy things has changed a lot. Online shopping allows people to buy products at home 
without visiting stores. This is fast and convenient. 
People can compare prices easily and read reviews before buying. Mobile payment also makes shopping 
quicker. 
So, technology has made buying easier, faster, and more flexible than before. 
 
Question 4: What do you think influences people to buy new things? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从情绪、广告和社会影响三方面展开，解释非理性消费的常见原因。 
Sample Answer: 
Many things influence people to buy new items. One main reason is emotion. When people feel bored or 
stressed, shopping can make them feel better for a short time. 
Advertising also has a strong effect. Sales, discounts, and attractive ads make people believe they need 
something new. Social media and friends’ choices can also influence decisions. 
So, emotions, marketing, and social influence often lead people to buy things they may not really need.

对家庭重要的东西 
Describe something important that has been kept in your family for a long time 
You should say: 
What it is 
When your family had it 
How your family got it 
And explain why it is important to your family 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“物品类 + 家庭记忆类”话题，要求你描述一件在你家里保存了很长时间的重要物品。需要说明：这件东
西是什么、你家是什么时候拥有它的、它是如何得到的，以及为什么它对你的家庭很重要。整体以过去时介绍来源
和历史，用现在时解释意义和情感。重点在于家庭情感和象征意义，而不是物品本身的价值。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择有纪念意义的老物件，比如手表、照片、家具或信件。思路上可以先说清这件物品是什么；然后可以
说一说家里是在什么时候、通过什么方式得到它的；接着重点可以放在它和家庭成员之间的故事；最后说明它为什
么对你们家来说很重要。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这件物品是什么，以及家里保存它多久了； 
第二段：说明家里是如何得到它的，并简单讲相关背景； 
第三段：解释它的重要性以及你对它的感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The item is an old wristwatch. 这件东西是一块老手表。 
My family has kept it for decades. 我家已经保存它几十年了。 
It has been passed down through generations. 它是一代一代传下来的。 
It belongs to my grandfather. 它原本属于我爷爷。 
It is still kept carefully at home. 它现在仍被仔细地保存着。 
具体描述 
My grandfather got it when he was young. 我爷爷年轻时得到了它。 
It was a gift from a close family member. 那是来自亲人的礼物。 
The watch has a simple design. 这块手表设计很简单。 
Although it is old, it still works. 虽然很旧，但还能用。 
It carries many family memories. 它承载了很多家庭记忆。 
描述感受 
It reminds us of our family history. 它让我们想起家庭的历史。 
It has strong emotional value. 它有很强的情感价值。 
I feel connected to my family when I see it. 看到它我会感到与家人更亲近。 
It teaches me to respect the past. 它让我学会尊重过去。 
That is why it is important to my family. 这就是它对我家重要的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Something important that has been kept in my family for a long time is an old wristwatch that belonged to my 
grandfather. My family has kept it for several decades, and it is still carefully stored at home. Even though it 
does not look very special at first glance, it means a lot to us. 
My grandfather got this watch when he was a young man. It was a gift from one of his close family members 
before he started working. He wore it almost every day for many years, especially during important moments 
in his life. After he passed away, the watch was kept by my parents as a family memory. Although it is quite old 
now, it still works, and the design is simple and classic. 
 

=== PAGE 73 ===
 
 
73 
 
 
This watch is important to my family because it connects us to our past. It reminds us of my grandfather’s hard 
work and his role in supporting the family. Every time I see it, I feel a strong sense of respect and closeness to 
my family history. It is not valuable in terms of money, but it has deep emotional value. That is why my family 
has kept it for such a long time and will continue to protect it in the future. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: What things do families keep for a long time? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从“情感价值”“家庭传承”“实用与纪念并存”三个角度展开，解释为什么这些
物品被长期保留，而不是因为价格本身。 
Sample Answer: 
Families often keep things that have special meaning. Photos, letters, and diaries are common because they 
record important memories and family history. Many families also keep jewelry or watches passed down from 
grandparents. 
Some people keep old furniture or books because they remind them of home and childhood. These items may 
not be expensive, but they connect family members across time. 
So, families keep things mainly for emotional value, memories, and a sense of tradition, not just for practical 
use. 
 
Question 2: What’s the difference between things valued by people in the past and today? 
解题思路：对比类问题。可以从生活条件、社会发展和价值观变化来展开，对比过去更重视稳定与实用，而今
天更重视个人感受与选择空间。 
Sample Answer: 
People in the past valued stability and basic needs more. They cared a lot about food, housing, and steady jobs 
because life was not easy. Family duty and saving money were also very important. 
Today, many people value personal happiness and freedom more. They care about interests, quality of life, and 
self-development. Experiences like travel and hobbies are seen as important. 
So, the main difference is that people in the past focused on survival and security, while people today care 
more about personal choice and enjoyment. 
 
Question 3: What kinds of things are kept in museums? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从博物馆的功能出发，分类说明常见展品类型，比如历史、艺术和科学相关物
品。重点解释这些物品为什么有保存价值，而不是只罗列名称。 
Sample Answer: 
Museums keep many kinds of valuable things. History museums often display old tools, clothes, coins, and 
objects used in daily life in the past. These items help people understand how people lived before. 
Art museums keep paintings, sculptures, and photos created by artists. Science museums show machines, 
models, and inventions that explain how things work. Some museums also keep animal bones or plants. 
So, museums keep objects that have historical, cultural, or educational value for the public. 
 
Question 4: What’s the influence of technology on museums? 
解题思路：影响类问题。可以从“展示方式”“参观方式”“学习效果”三个方面展开，重点解释科技如何让博
物馆更容易被理解和接近，而不是只强调技术本身有多先进。 
Sample Answer: 
Technology has changed museums in many ways. Today, museums use screens, videos, and audio guides to 
explain exhibits more clearly. This helps visitors understand history and culture without reading long texts. 
Technology also allows people to visit museums online. Virtual tours are helpful for students and people who 
cannot travel far. Interactive displays make museums more interesting, especially for children. 
So, technology makes museums more modern, accessible, and enjoyable, and it helps more people learn from 
them. 
 
 

=== PAGE 74 ===
 
 
74 
 
 
 
花费超过预期的物品 
Describe an item on which you spent more than expected 
You should say: 
What it is 
How much you spent on it 
Why you bought it 
And explain why you think you spent more than expected 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“物品类 + 反思类”题目，要求你描述一次花费超出预期的购物经历。题目核心不在于“贵”，而在于
“为什么会超出原本的计划”。你需要说明购买的是什么、实际花了多少钱、购买动机，以及你事后对这次消费的
看法。整体时态以过去时为主，感受和反思部分可以使用现在时。 
思路方面 
可以选择生活中比较真实、容易展开的消费场景，比如电子产品、衣服、课程、旅行或家具等。重点放在“本来怎
么想的”和“最后为什么多花了钱”，原因可以是质量更好、配置升级、促销诱导或当时的情绪影响。最后要体现
出你的理性反思，而不是单纯后悔。 
结构方面 
第一段介绍你买了什么东西，以及大概的花费情况。 
第二段说明你当初为什么要买它，以及原本的预算是什么。 
第三段解释为什么最后花得更多，并补充你对这次消费的感受和看法 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It happened about a year ago. 这件事发生在大约一年前。 
I didn’t plan to spend that much at first. 起初并没打算花这么多钱。 
I had a clear budget in mind. 我原本心里是有预算的。 
It was something I had wanted for a long time. 这是我想要很久的一样东西。 
I bought it during a shopping season. 我是在购物季买的。 
具体描述 
I ended up paying nearly 5,000 yuan. 最后我花了将近五千元。 
I upgraded to a better version. 我升级成了更高配的版本。 
The salesperson strongly recommended it. 销售人员强烈推荐了它。 
The quality was much better than the cheaper option. 它的质量明显比便宜的版本好。 
There were extra features I didn’t expect to need. 有一些我原本没打算要的功能。 
描述感受 
I felt a bit shocked when I saw the final price. 看到最终价格时我有点震惊。 
At the same time, I felt it was worth it. 同时我也觉得它是值得的。 
It taught me to think more carefully before spending. 这件事让我学会更理性消费。 
I became more aware of my spending habits. 我开始更关注自己的消费习惯。 
Looking back, I don’t regret the decision. 回头看，我并不后悔这个决定。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Last year, I spent much more than expected on a pair of wireless noise-cancelling headphones. Originally, I 
planned to spend around 2,000 yuan, but in the end, I paid nearly 4,000 yuan for a higher-end model. 
I bought them because I needed something to help me focus while studying and traveling. I often work in noisy 
environments, and I wanted better sound quality and comfort. At first, I was looking at a basic version, but after 
trying several models in the store, I noticed a big difference in performance. The more expensive version had 
stronger noise reduction, clearer sound, and a longer battery life. 
 

=== PAGE 75 ===
 
 
75 
 
 
 
What really made me spend more than expected was a mix of comparison and persuasion. The salesperson 
explained the extra features in detail, and I started to feel that the cheaper option wouldn’t last long. Although 
I felt a bit surprised when I saw the final price, I also felt satisfied afterward. Using these headphones has 
improved my daily routine, and I don’t regret the purchase. Still, the experience reminded me to be more 
careful with my budget in the future. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Do you often buy more than you expected? 
解题思路：个人态度与原因类问题。可以承认“偶尔会”，并解释促销、情绪和便利性如何影响消费。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, sometimes I buy more than I expected. When I see discounts or special offers, I feel it is a good chance and 
add extra items. 
Emotions also matter. After a busy day, shopping can feel relaxing, so I may buy things I don’t really need. 
Online shopping makes this easier because it is fast and convenient. 
However, I try to control myself by making lists and thinking before paying. So, while it happens, I am learning 
to shop more carefully. 
 
Question 2: What do you think young people spend most of their money on? 
解题思路：说明与原因类问题。可以从生活方式和消费习惯展开，解释年轻人把钱花在娱乐、电子产品和社交
上的原因，而不是简单列举项目。 
Sample Answer: 
I think young people spend most of their money on daily life and enjoyment. Many pay for food, rent, and 
transport, especially in big cities. 
They also spend a lot on phones, clothes, and online shopping. Entertainment is another big part, such as 
movies, games, and travel. These things help them relax and connect with friends. 
Young people like trying new products and experiences, which also costs money. So, most of their spending is 
related to living needs, social life, and personal enjoyment. 
 
Question 3: Do you think it is important to save money? Why? 
解题思路：观点 + 原因类问题。可以从安全感、未来规划和习惯培养解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, saving money is important. It helps people feel safe when unexpected problems happen, such as illness or 
job change. 
Saving also helps people plan for the future, like buying a house or traveling. It teaches self-control and 
responsibility. 
So, saving money is not about being cheap, but about being prepared and confident. 
 
Question 4: Do people buy things they don’t need? 
解题思路：事实 + 原因类问题。可以直接回答“是的”，并解释原因。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, many people buy things they don’t really need. This often happens because of sales or online shopping. 
When prices look low, people feel it is a good chance to buy more. 
Emotions also play a role. Shopping can be relaxing and enjoyable, especially after a busy day. People may buy 
items just because they look nice. 
So, buying unnecessary things is common due to emotions and strong marketing. 
 
 

=== PAGE 76 ===
 
 
76 
 
 
有趣的建筑 
Describe an interesting building 
You should say: 
Where it is 
What it looks like 
What function it has 
And explain why you think it is interesting 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“物品类 + 观点类”题目，要求你介绍一座你觉得有趣的建筑。题目关注四个要点：建筑的位置、外观、
功能，以及你认为它有趣的原因。整体时态以一般现在时为主，在提及历史背景或个人经历时可使用过去时。 
思路方面 
可以选择一座外观独特、功能明确、知名度较高的建筑，方便展开描述。重点不在技术细节，而在于造型、用途与
个人感受之间的联系。你可以从设计灵感、使用场景或它带来的城市印象入手，说明“为什么有趣”。 
结构方面 
第一段交代建筑的位置和基本背景。 
第二段描述建筑外观与主要功能。 
第三段解释你认为它有趣的原因，并补充你的情感态度 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
It is located in the northern part of the city. 位于城市的北部。 
It has become a city landmark. 它已经成为城市地标。 
Many major events are held there. 许多大型活动在这里举行。 
It attracts visitors from around the world. 吸引了来自世界各地的游客。 
The building was designed for public use. 这座建筑是为公众使用而设计的。 
具体描述 
The structure looks like a giant nest made of steel. 整体结构看起来像由钢材组成的巨大鸟巢。 
The design is both modern and symbolic. 设计既现代又富有象征意义。 
It has a large open space inside. 内部空间非常开阔。 
The building is mainly used for sports events. 这座建筑主要用于体育赛事。 
It can also host concerts and shows. 它也可以举办演唱会和表演。 
描述感受 
I find it visually striking. 我觉得它在视觉上非常震撼。 
It left a deep impression on me. 它给我留下了深刻印象。 
It represents creativity and ambition. 它代表了创造力和雄心。 
I feel proud when talking about it. 提到它时我感到很自豪。 
It makes the city feel more dynamic. 它让这座城市更有活力。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Located in Beijing, Beijing National Stadium, also known as the Bird’s Nest, is an interesting building that always 
catches my attention. It stands in the Olympic Park and has become one of the most recognizable landmarks in 
the city. 
The building looks like a huge nest made from interwoven steel beams. From the outside, the structure 
appears complex and artistic, while the inside is surprisingly open and spacious. Its design is modern, but at the 
same time, it feels natural and symbolic. The stadium is mainly used for large sports events, but it also hosts 
concerts and public activities, which makes it very practical. 
What makes this building especially interesting to me is how it combines creativity with function. It’s not just a 
place for events; it also represents innovation and confidence. Every time I see it, I feel impressed by the bold 

=== PAGE 77 ===
 
 
77 
 
 
design and the ideas behind it. The Bird’s Nest adds character to the city and shows how architecture can be 
both useful and inspiring. 
Part 3  
Question 1: What types of buildings are popular in your country? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从城市化、生活方式和需求解释不同建筑类型的流行原因。 
Sample Answer: 
In my country, apartment buildings are very popular, especially in cities. They save space and are close to 
schools, shops, and transport. Many families choose apartments for convenience. 
In suburban or rural areas, houses are also common. People like them because they offer more space and 
privacy. 
Shopping malls and office buildings are also popular due to business growth. 
So, building types depend on location, lifestyle, and daily needs. 
 
Question 2: Is it worth spending a lot of money on the exterior appearance of a building? 
解题思路：评估类问题。可以采取中立立场，说明外观重要但不应超过功能和安全。 
Sample Answer: 
I think spending some money on a building’s exterior is worth it, but not too much. A nice appearance makes a 
city more pleasant and creates a good first impression. 
However, function and safety are more important. If too much money is spent on looks, basic needs like 
comfort or safety may be ignored. 
So, exterior design matters, but it should be balanced with practical use and long-term value. 
 
Question 3: Is it more important for a building to look good on the outside or on the inside? 
解题思路：评估类问题。可以给出“内部更重要”的观点，并解释原因。 
Sample Answer: 
I think the inside of a building is more important. People use the inside every day, so comfort, safety, and 
function matter most. 
A nice outside can attract attention, but it is less useful if the inside is uncomfortable. 
So, appearance is important, but practical use should come first. 
 
Question 4: Why do people like to visit historical sites? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从学习、文化认同和体验感展开。 
Sample Answer: 
People like to visit historical sites because they want to learn about the past. Seeing old buildings and places 
helps history feel real. 
Historical sites also give people a sense of culture and identity. They help people understand where they come 
from. Many sites are also beautiful and peaceful. 
So, people visit historical sites to learn, feel connected to history, and enjoy special experiences.

App or 程序 
Describe a program or app on your computer or phone 
You should say: 
What it is 
How often you use it 
When or how you use it 
When or how you found it 
And explain how you feel about it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“抽象物品+科技类”话题，要求你描述一个你电脑或手机上常用的程序或应用。题目需要你说清：它是
什么、你多久用一次、你在什么情况下使用它、你是如何发现它的，以及你对它的感受。整体以现在时描述使用习
惯，用过去时补充发现过程。重点在于真实使用场景和个人体验。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择你生活中真实常用的 app，比如学习、记录、娱乐或沟通类。思路上可以先说清这个 app 是什么；然
后要说清你使用它的频率；接着可以重点说你在什么时间或什么情况下会用它；再补充你是如何发现它的；最后说
明你对它的整体感受。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍这个 app 是什么，以及你是如何发现它的； 
第二段：描述你使用它的频率和具体使用方式； 
第三段：解释你对这个 app 的感受，并总结它对你生活的影响。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
The app I want to talk about is Notion. 我想说的这个应用是 Notion。 
I use it on both my phone and computer. 我在手机和电脑上都用它。 
I found it through a friend. 我是通过朋友知道它的。 
I started using it last year. 我是去年开始用它的。 
It is a very useful tool for me. 它对我来说是一个很有用的工具。 
具体描述 
I use it almost every day. 我几乎每天都会用它。 
I use it to write notes and plans. 我用它来记笔记和做计划。 
I usually use it in the evening. 我通常在晚上用它。 
I open it when I need to organize my work. 我需要整理事情时就会打开它。 
It helps me keep things clear. 它帮我把事情理清楚。 
描述感受 
It makes me feel more organized. 它让我更有条理。 
I feel less stressed when using it. 用它的时候我压力更小。 
It is easy to use and simple. 它简单也容易用。 
I feel comfortable relying on it. 我很习惯依赖它。 
That is why I really like this app. 这就是我很喜欢它的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A program I often use on my computer and phone is an app called Notion. I first found it last year through a 
friend who used it for study and daily planning. At that time, I was looking for a simple way to organize my 
notes and tasks, so I decided to try it. 
 
 

=== PAGE 79 ===
 
 
79 
 
 
I use this app almost every day. I usually open it in the evening when I want to review my day or plan for the 
next one. I use it to write short notes, make to-do lists, and organize my work in a clear way. Sometimes I also 
use it during the day when an idea suddenly comes to my mind. Because it works on both my phone and 
computer, I can use it anywhere and anytime, which is very convenient. 
I feel very positive about this app because it helps me stay organized and calm. Before using it, I often forgot 
things or felt stressed about unfinished tasks. Now, I can see everything clearly in one place. The design is 
simple, and it does not make me feel tired when using it for a long time. This app has become part of my daily 
routine, and I feel more in control of my time and work. That is why I really like using Notion and would 
recommend it to others who want to live in a more organized way. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: What are the differences between old and young people when using apps? 
解题思路：对比类问题。可以从“目的”“使用频率”“熟练度”来展开，并解释背后的原因。 
Sample Answer: 
Young people usually use apps more often and for many purposes, like social media, games, and shopping. 
They learn new apps quickly and enjoy trying new functions. 
Older people mainly use apps for communication, news, or payments. They prefer simple apps and may need 
more time to learn. 
So, the main difference is how often and how confidently they use apps. 
 
Question 2: Why do some people not like using apps? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“操作复杂”“隐私担忧”“不习惯科技”三个角度展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Some people do not like using apps because they find them difficult to use. New apps often change quickly, 
which can confuse users. 
Others worry about privacy and personal information, especially when apps ask for access to contacts or 
photos. Older people may also prefer traditional ways, like face-to-face service. 
So, dislike for apps often comes from habit, safety concerns, and lack of confidence with technology. 
 
Question 3: What apps are popular in your country? Why? 
解题思路：说明 + 原因类问题。可以从社交、娱乐和生活服务类应用展开，并解释受欢迎原因。 
Sample Answer: 
In my country, social media apps are very popular. People use them to chat, share photos, and follow news. 
Video apps are also common because they are relaxing and fun. 
Payment and shopping apps are widely used as well. They make daily life more convenient, such as paying bills 
or buying food. 
These apps are popular because they save time and fit modern lifestyles. 
 
Question 4: Should parents limit their children’s use of computer programs and computer games? Why and 
how? 
解题思路：观点 + 方法类问题。需要解释“为什么要限制”，以及“如何合理限制”，而不是简单禁止。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, parents should limit children’s use of computer programs and games. Too much screen time can affect 
health, study, and sleep. Children may become less active or lose focus. 
However, computers are also useful for learning. Parents should set clear time limits and choose suitable 
programs. They can encourage children to take breaks and do outdoor activities. 
So, limiting use in a balanced way helps children enjoy technology without negative effects.

最近读过的故事 
Describe a story (e.g. a fairy tale, etc.) you have read recently 
You should say: 
What it is about  
When you read it 
Whether you liked it 
And explain what you have learned from it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“抽象物品+故事类”话题，要求你描述最近读过的一则故事。题目需要你说明：故事讲什么、什么时候
读的、你是否喜欢，以及你从中学到了什么。整体以过去时讲经历，用现在时总结感受和启发。重点不在故事复杂
度，而在理解和个人收获。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择童话、寓言或短篇故事。思路上要说清：故事的核心内容和人物冲突；然后可以说一说你读完后的态
度，是喜欢还是一般；最后重点可以放在你从故事中学到的道理，比如勇气、善良、坚持或诚实。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍故事是什么，以及你什么时候读到的； 
第二段：简单讲故事内容，并说明你是否喜欢； 
第三段：解释你从故事中学到了什么，以及你的感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
I read this story recently in my free time. 我最近在空闲时间读了这个故事。 
It is a short fairy tale. 它是一则短小的童话故事。 
I came across it online. 我是在网上看到它的。 
I read it before going to bed. 我是在睡前读的。 
It did not take long to finish. 这个故事不长，很快就读完了。 
具体描述 
The story is about a young girl and her journey. 故事讲的是一个小女孩的经历。 
The main character faces many difficulties. 主人公遇到了很多困难。 
She learns to be brave and kind. 她学会了勇敢和善良。 
The story is simple but meaningful. 故事很简单，但很有意义。 
It has a clear message. 它的寓意很清楚。 
描述感受 
I really enjoyed reading it. 我很享受读这个故事。 
It made me think about my own life. 它让我思考自己的生活。 
I learned an important lesson from it. 我从中学到了重要的一课。 
The story left a deep impression on me. 这个故事给我留下了深刻印象。 
It reminded me to stay positive. 它提醒我要保持积极。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A story I read recently is a short fairy tale called The Little Match Girl. I read it about a month ago when I was 
looking for something simple to read before going to bed. I had heard about this story before, but this was the 
first time I read it carefully from beginning to end. 
The story is about a poor little girl who sells matches on a cold winter night. She lights matches to keep herself 
warm and sees beautiful visions, such as food, warmth, and love. Sadly, her life is very difficult, and the story 
ends in a touching way. Even though the story is short and the language is simple, it made me feel emotional. I 
did like the story, but it was not a happy one. It was meaningful and made me slow down and think. 
 
 

=== PAGE 81 ===
 
 
81 
 
 
From this story, I learned to be more thankful for what I have. It reminded me that many people live hard lives, 
and kindness is very important. I also learned that stories do not need to be long or complex to be powerful. 
This fairy tale helped me see life from a different angle, and that is why I still remember it clearly after reading 
it. 
Part 3  
Question 1: Why do most children like listening to stories before bedtime? 
解题思路：原因类问题。可以从“安全感”“想象力”“亲子关系”三个角度解释。 
Sample Answer: 
Children like bedtime stories because they feel relaxed and safe. Listening to stories helps them calm down 
before sleep. 
Stories also bring imagination, with animals, heroes, and adventures. When parents read stories, children feel 
loved and cared for. 
So, bedtime stories help children feel peaceful, happy, and ready to sleep. 
 
Question 2: Is a good storyline important for a movie? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“理解”“情感投入”“观影体验”解释剧情的重要性。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, a good storyline is very important for a movie. A clear story helps the audience understand what is 
happening and stay interested. 
Without a good storyline, even great actors or special effects cannot hold attention for long. A strong story also 
helps people connect emotionally with characters. 
So, a good storyline makes a movie meaningful and enjoyable, not just visually attractive. 
 
Question 3: Do you think films with many celebrities are more likely to be popular? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以先承认明星效应的吸引力，再强调内容的重要性。 
Sample Answer: 
Films with many celebrities are often popular at first because famous actors attract attention. People are 
curious and want to see their favorite stars. 
However, popularity does not last if the story is weak. Audiences care about storyline and emotions. A good 
movie needs more than famous faces. 
So, celebrities help, but story and quality matter more in the long run. 
 
Question 4: What films are popular in China right now? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以列举几类电影并简单说明受欢迎原因。 
Sample Answer: 
In China, several types of films are popular now. Action films and family films attract large audiences because 
they are exciting or emotional. 
Comedy films are also popular, as people enjoy relaxing and laughing after work. In recent years, historical and 
patriotic films have gained attention because they tell meaningful stories. 
So, popular films in China usually mix entertainment, emotion, and cultural themes.

让你失望的电影 
Describe a movie you watched recently that you felt disappointed about 
You should say: 
When it was 
Why you didn’t like it 
Why you decided to watch it 
And explain why you felt disappointed about it 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是“抽象物品 + 观点感受类”话题，要求你描述最近看过的一部让你失望的电影。需要说明：什么时候看的、你
为什么不喜欢、你为什么会决定去看、以及为什么会感到失望。整体叙述以过去时为主，最后总结感受可用现在
时。重点在于期待与实际体验的落差。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择一部宣传很火、评分看起来不错、但观影体验一般的电影。思路上可以先说清你是在什么情况下看
的；然后可以重点说你原本的期待从哪里来；接着说一说电影中让你不满意的地方，比如剧情、节奏或人物；最后
说明这种落差为什么让你失望。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍你什么时候看了这部电影，以及为什么决定去看； 
第二段：描述你不喜欢的具体原因； 
第三段：解释你为什么感到失望，并总结你的感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
I watched this movie last month. 我是上个月看的这部电影。 
I decided to watch it with my friends. 我是和朋友一起决定看的。 
It was very popular at that time. 它在当时非常火。 
I saw many positive reviews online. 我在网上看到了很多好评。 
I had high expectations before watching it. 看之前我期待很高。 
具体描述 
The story was slow and confusing. 剧情又慢又有点乱。 
The characters did not feel real. 人物不够真实。 
Some scenes felt unnecessary. 有些情节显得多余。 
The ending was not satisfying. 结尾让人不太满意。 
I felt bored during some parts of the movie. 电影有些地方让我觉得无聊。 
描述感受 
I felt disappointed after it ended. 看完后我感到失望。 
It was not as good as I expected. 它没有我想象中那么好。 
The experience made me more careful about choosing movies. 这次经历让我以后选电影更谨慎。 
I wished it could have been better. 我真希望它能更好一点。 
Overall, it did not leave a good impression on me. 总体来说，它没给我留下好印象。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A movie I watched recently that made me feel disappointed was Wonder Woman 1984. I watched it about a 
month ago at home with my friends. At that time, the movie was still being talked about online, and many 
people said it was exciting and meaningful, so I decided to give it a try. 
I chose to watch this movie because I liked the first Wonder Woman film and expected something similar. I also 
enjoy superhero movies in general, because they are usually full of action and strong characters.  

=== PAGE 83 ===
 
 
83 
 
 
However, after watching it, I found the story slow and sometimes confusing. Some scenes felt too long, and the 
main characters did not develop in a clear way. I also felt that the ending was not very satisfying, and some 
parts did not make sense to me. During the movie, I even felt bored at times, which surprised me. 
I felt disappointed because my expectations were quite high. I thought the movie would be powerful and 
inspiring, but it did not meet that standard. It was not terrible, but it was far from what I hoped for. This 
experience taught me that popular movies are not always good, and reviews do not always match personal 
taste. Overall, the movie did not leave a strong impression on me, and that is why I felt disappointed after 
watching it.

Question 1: Do you believe movie reviews?

However, different people have different tastes, so reviews are not always accurate. Some reviews may also be 
paid or exaggerated. 
So, I read reviews as a reference, but I prefer to decide after watching the movie myself. 
 
Question 2: What are the different types of films in your country?

There are also romantic films, family films, and historical movies. Some people enjoy science fiction, while

So, film types are diverse, and people choose based on mood and interest. 
 
Question 3: Are historical films popular in your country? Why?

Sample Answer: 
Yes, historical films are quite popular in my country. They tell stories about the past and help people 
understand history and culture. 
Many people enjoy learning while watching movies. Historical films also bring national pride and emotional 
connection. 
So, these films are popular because they educate, entertain, and connect people with history. 
 
Question 4: Do you think films with famous actors or actresses are more likely to become successful films? 
解题思路：评估类问题。可以先承认明星效应，再强调内容质量。 
Sample Answer:

ticket sales. 
However, long-term success depends on the story and quality. If the plot is weak, audiences may feel 
disappointed. 
So, famous actors help at first, but a good film needs more than stars.

完美工作 
Describe a perfect job you would like to have in the future 
You should say: 
What it is 
How you knew it 
What you need to learn to get this job  
And explain why you think it is a perfect job for you 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“抽象物品+工作类”话题，要求你描述一份你将来想拥有的理想工作。题目需要你说清：这份工作是什
么、你是如何了解到这份工作的、为了得到这份工作你需要学习什么，以及为什么你认为它非常适合你。整体以将
来时和现在时为主，介绍了解过程时可用过去时。重点在于个人兴趣与工作的匹配度。 
思路方面 
这里可以选择一份与你性格和能力相关的工作。思路上可以先说清这份工作的基本内容；然后可以说你是在什么情
况下认识或了解这份工作的；接着要说清为了胜任这份工作你需要学习哪些技能；最后可以重点说这份工作为什么
适合你，比如生活方式、成就感或长期发展。 
结构方面 
第一段：介绍你理想的工作是什么，以及你是如何了解到它的； 
第二段：说明为了得到这份工作你需要学习和准备的内容； 
第三段：解释为什么你认为这份工作是你的完美工作，并总结你的感受。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
My perfect job is being a content creator. 我理想的工作是做内容创作者。 
I learned about this job through the internet. 我是通过网络了解这份工作的。 
It is closely related to my interests. 它和我的兴趣密切相关。 
This job is becoming more popular. 这份工作越来越受欢迎。 
I have thought about it for a long time. 我已经考虑这份工作很久了。 
具体描述 
I need to improve my writing skills. 我需要提升写作能力。 
I also need to learn basic design skills. 我还需要学习基础设计技能。 
Time management is very important. 时间管理非常重要。 
I need to learn how to communicate clearly. 我需要学习清晰地表达。 
Practical experience matters a lot. 实际经验非常重要。 
描述感受 
This job allows me to be creative. 这份工作让我有创造空间。 
I can share ideas with others. 我可以和别人分享想法。 
It fits my personality well. 它很符合我的性格。 
I believe I would enjoy doing it. 我相信我会享受这份工作。 
That is why I think it is perfect for me. 这就是我认为它适合我的原因。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
A perfect job I would like to have in the future is being a content creator. I learned about this job mainly 
through the internet and social media. At first, I followed some people who shared useful ideas and daily 
experiences online. Over time, I realized that creating content is not only about entertainment, but also about 
communication and influence. 
To get this job, I need to learn several important skills. First, I need to improve my writing and speaking skills, 
because clear expression is the key to good content. I also need to learn some basic design and video editing 
skills, so that my work can look more attractive.  

=== PAGE 85 ===
 
 
85 
 
 
In addition, time management is very important, since content creators usually work on their own and need to 
plan their time carefully. Practical experience also matters a lot, so I believe I need to keep practicing and 
learning from feedback. 
I think this job is perfect for me because it fits my personality and interests very well. I enjoy sharing ideas and 
connecting with people. This job allows me to be creative and flexible, instead of doing the same thing every 
day. It also gives me a sense of achievement when my work helps or inspires others. For these reasons, I 
believe being a content creator would be a job I truly enjoy and want to work toward in the future. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: What kind of job can be called a ‘dream job’? 
解题思路：说明与观点类问题。可以从“兴趣匹配”“成就感”“生活平衡”展开，解释为什么理想工作不仅是
高薪，更是长期满意度 
Sample Answer: 
A dream job is a job that fits a person’s interests and values. People enjoy their work and feel motivated every 
day. They feel proud of what they do and see meaning in their tasks. 
A dream job also offers balance. It allows time for family and rest, not only long hours. Some people value 
learning chances and growth more than money. 
So, a dream job is not the same for everyone. It is a job that brings happiness, purpose, and a comfortable life 
style. 
 
Question 2: What jobs do children want to do when they grow up? 
解题思路：说明类问题。可以从“理想化”“榜样影响”展开。 
Sample Answer: 
Children often want to do interesting jobs, like doctors, teachers, or police officers. Some want to be singers, 
actors, or athletes. 
These jobs look exciting and meaningful to them. Children are often influenced by parents, TV, and people they 
admire. 
So, children choose jobs based on dreams and imagination. 
 
Question 3: Do people’s ideal jobs change as they grow up? 
解题思路：变化类问题。可以从年龄增长、现实经验和责任变化来解释为什么理想职业会发生改变。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, people’s ideal jobs often change as they grow up. When people are young, they choose jobs based on 
dreams or interests, like being a singer or athlete. 
As they grow older, they think more about reality. Salary, stability, and work-life balance become important, 
especially when they have family duties. Experience also helps people understand what suits them. 
So, ideal jobs change because people’s needs, responsibilities, and understanding of life change over time. 
 
Question 4: What should people consider when choosing jobs? 
解题思路：说明 + 原因类问题。可以从兴趣、能力、收入、工作环境等角度展开。 
Sample Answer: 
When choosing jobs, people should consider interest first. Enjoying the job helps them stay motivated. 
They should also think about skills and ability, because a job should match what they can do well. Income and 
work-life balance are important too. 
So, choosing a job needs careful thought about both personal needs and practical factors. 
 
 

=== PAGE 86 ===
 
 
86 
 
 
朋友所学 
Describe one of your friends who learned something new (not from a teacher) 
You should say: 
Who he or she is 
What he or she learned 
Why he or she learned this 
And explain whether it would be easier to learn from a teacher 
 
教师的解析： 
审题方面 
这是一道“人物 + 学习经历”的题目，核心在于描述一位朋友在没有老师指导的情况下学会了一项新技能。题目不
仅要求你说明他或她是谁、学了什么、为什么学，还要求你进一步评价“如果有老师，是否会更容易”。因此，内
容既包括事实描述，也需要加入你的个人看法。整体时态以过去时为主，在评价学习方式时可以使用现在时。 
思路方面 
你可以选择一位身边真实的朋友，比如自学摄影、剪辑、健身、做饭、编程或乐器等。重点不在技能难度，而在
“自学过程”。你可以描述他/她是通过网络视频、反复练习或兴趣驱动来学习的，并简单提到遇到的困难。最后再
对比一下：如果有老师，是否会更系统，但自学是否也有独特优势。 
结构方面 
第一段介绍这位朋友是谁，以及他或她学会了什么新技能。 
第二段重点描述他或她为什么学习这项技能，以及具体是如何自学的。 
第三段讨论你对这种学习方式的看法，并回答是否有老师会更容易，同时给出你的理由。 
 
答题参考 
背景描述： 
He is a close friend of mine from university. 他是我大学里的一位好朋友。 
I’ve known him for several years. 我认识他已经好几年了。 
We often share similar hobbies. 我们有很多相似的兴趣爱好。 
He decided to learn something new on his own. 他决定自学一项新技能。 
This happened about a year ago. 这件事发生在大约一年前。 
具体描述 
He taught himself video editing. 他自学了视频剪辑。 
He learned it through online tutorials and practice. 他通过网络教程和反复练习来学习。 
He wanted to improve his creative skills. 他想提升自己的创造力。 
He spent a lot of time experimenting and making mistakes. 他花了很多时间尝试和犯错。 
Gradually, he became more confident with this skill. 慢慢地，他对这项技能越来越有信心。 
描述感受 
 
I really admire his self-discipline. 我很佩服他的自律。 
Learning without a teacher takes strong motivation. 没有老师的学习需要很强的动力。 
A teacher could make the learning process faster. 老师可能会让学习过程更高效。 
Self-learning also allows more freedom. 自学也带来了更多自由。 
I think both ways have their advantages. 我觉得两种方式各有优势。 
 
Sample Answer  ： 
Back in university, I had a close friend named Eric who decided to learn video editing completely on his own. 
He wasn’t studying media or design, but he became interested in editing because he wanted to make short 
videos for social media and record his daily life in a more creative way. 
Instead of taking classes, he relied on online tutorials, forums, and a lot of trial and error. He spent many 
evenings watching editing videos and then practicing on his laptop.  
 
 

=== PAGE 87 ===
 
 
87 
 
 
At first, it was slow and frustrating, but over time, his skills improved a lot. He learned because of pure interest, 
not pressure, which kept him motivated. 
In my opinion, learning from a teacher would probably be easier in some ways, especially for learning 
techniques more quickly. However, self-learning gave him more freedom and confidence, and he could move at 
his own pace. I really admire his determination, and his experience showed me that learning doesn’t always 
need a classroom. 
 
Part 3  
Question 1: Is it necessary to keep learning after graduating from school? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从“社会变化快”“工作需要”“个人成长”解释为什么毕业后学习仍然重要。 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, it is necessary to keep learning after graduating from school. Knowledge and skills change quickly in 
modern society, especially at work. People need to learn new tools and ideas to stay useful. 
Learning also helps people grow personally. Reading, training, or learning new hobbies keeps the mind active 
and confident. It can also bring new chances in life. 
So, learning should not stop at graduation. It is a lifelong process that helps people adapt and improve. 
 
Question 2: Should teachers make learning in their classes fun? 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以从学习动机、课堂参与度和学习效果来解释“有趣教学”的意义，同时强调“有
趣不等于不严肃” 
Sample Answer: 
Yes, teachers should make learning fun in class. When lessons are interesting, students pay more attention and 
feel less pressure. Fun activities help students remember knowledge more easily. 
Enjoyable classes also encourage students to ask questions and join discussions. This builds confidence and 
interest in learning. However, fun should support learning goals, not replace them. 
So, making learning fun helps students stay motivated and learn better when it is done in a balanced way. 
 
Question 3: Do you think there are too many subjects for students to learn? 
 
解题思路：观点类问题。可以承认学习负担存在，同时解释多学科的价值。 
Sample Answer: 
I think some students do have too many subjects to learn. Heavy study pressure can make them feel tired and 
stressed. 
However, learning different subjects helps students build basic knowledge and discover interests. The problem 
is not the number of subjects, but how they are taught. 
So, balance is important. Students need enough subjects, but also enough rest and focus. 
 
Question 4: Is it better to focus on a few subjects or to learn many subjects? 
解题思路：对比类问题。可以给出“阶段不同，选择不同”的观点，解释各自的优点。 
Sample Answer: 
I think it depends on the stage of learning. Learning many subjects helps students build a broad base and 
discover interests. It is especially useful when students are young. 
Focusing on a few subjects is better at a later stage. It helps students go deeper and build strong skills. Too 
many subjects can also cause stress. 
So, learning broadly first and then focusing later is a good balance for most people.
